var SHEET_ID = '1JlP7BUaD5qzN6hyunzhiuiHNII9AGA1StGL8_xRUFBU'; var WEBHOOK_URL = 'https://dc.jay87012205.workers.dev/api/webhooks/1474932936246558821/lho0Q1WRihhaRXZaaIvCiqAPIt54pTlAPV8-FyOkQFRdxSmqRw5mdx-YLP3O09fAZ6XB'; // 🌟 效能優化:Discord webhook 是網路請求,可能要幾百毫秒,如果在 LockService 鎖定期間發送, // 會讓其他人的出價/購買一起卡住排隊。改成「鎖定期間只收集要發的訊息,鎖一放開就馬上送出」, // 這樣鎖只用來保護試算表讀寫這種真正需要互斥的操作,不會被網路延遲拖慢。 var __pendingWebhooks = []; function queueWebhook_(msg) { __pendingWebhooks.push(msg); } function flushPendingWebhooks_() { var queue = __pendingWebhooks; __pendingWebhooks = []; for (var i = 0; i < queue.length; i++) { var msg = queue[i]; if (msg.length > 1900) msg = msg.substring(0, 1900) + " ... (內容過多已省略)"; // 🌟🔧 每一則訊息都是各自獨立的一次 HTTP 請求(不是合併成一則發送),Discord webhook 大約每2秒最多5次、 // 每分鐘上限也有限制,狂發一長串很容易踩到限流(收到 429)。這裡加兩層防護: // 1) 每則之間固定間隔一點點時間,降低一開始就踩到限流的機率 // 2) 萬一還是被限流(429),照 Discord 回傳的 Retry-After 指示等待後重試一次,不要直接放棄漏發 if (i > 0) Utilities.sleep(350); var sent = false; for (var attempt = 0; attempt < 2 && !sent; attempt++) { try { var resp = UrlFetchApp.fetch(WEBHOOK_URL, { "method": "post", "contentType": "application/json", "payload": JSON.stringify({ "content": msg }), "muteHttpExceptions": true }); var code = resp.getResponseCode(); if (code === 429) { var retryAfterSec = 1; try { var body = JSON.parse(resp.getContentText()); if (body && body.retry_after) retryAfterSec = Math.min(body.retry_after, 5); // 🌟 保險上限5秒,避免單一觸發器執行時間爆掉 } catch (pe) {} Utilities.sleep(retryAfterSec * 1000 + 100); continue; // 🌟 重試一次(attempt迴圈最多跑2次:第一次被限流、第二次補發) } sent = true; // 🌟 不管是200成功還是其他非429的錯誤,都當作處理完了,不要卡住整條佇列 } catch (e) { sent = true; // 🌟 網路層級的例外也直接放棄這一則,繼續發下一則,避免一則卡死整批 } } } } // 🌟 身分組限定功能設定 // 因為從 GAS/Cloudflare Worker 直接呼叫 Discord 受保護的 API 會被 Cloudflare 擋下(403 / code 40333), // 所以改成「由 Skript Bot 主動把使用者目前的身分組 ID 寫進玩家表」,GAS 只負責讀表,不再呼叫 Discord API。 // PLAYER_ROLE_COLUMN：玩家表中存放身分組ID的欄位名稱(逗號分隔多個ID),由 Skript Bot 透過 doPost 寫入 // ROLE_NAME_MAP_SHEET：身分組「ID -> 顯示名稱」對照表的工作表名稱(管理員手動維護,A欄=身分組ID, B欄=顯示名稱) var PLAYER_ROLE_COLUMN = 'DC身分組'; var PLAYER_NAME_COLUMN = 'DC暱稱'; // 🌟 玩家表裡存放Discord顯示名稱的欄位,由Skript Bot同步寫入,跟DC身分組是同一套機制 // 🌟 管理員 Discord ID 清單 — 跟 index.html 裡的 ADMIN_IDS 保持一致 var ADMIN_IDS = ['176681551189377024', '425655020017680395', '999888777666555444']; else if (action === 'buy') { var itemId = e.parameter.itemId; var qty = parseInt(e.parameter.qty) || 1; var altMode = e.parameter.altMode || 'none'; // 🌟 替代貨幣折抵模式: none(不使用) / auto(自動依序折抵) / manual(自訂各幣種數量) var altAmount = e.parameter.altAmount; // manual模式:JSON字串 {"幣種名稱":數量, ...} var altSelected = e.parameter.altSelected || ''; // 🌟 玩家這次選擇要用哪幾種替代貨幣,逗號分隔的幣種名稱清單 var unlockPassword = e.parameter.unlockPassword || ''; // 🌟 商品/分類密碼鎖定用 var gamblingOption = e.parameter.gamblingOption || ''; var shopSheet = ss.getSheets()[1]; var data = shopSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); var itemFound = null; for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) { if (data[i][18] && data[i][18].toString().trim() === itemId.toString()) { // ID 移到 S(18) itemFound = data[i]; break; } } var title = "Garbled 幻彩水晶商店"; var desc = "點擊進入商店查看豐富商品並兌換！"; var image = "https://discord.com/assets/2c21aeda16de354ba5334551a883b481.png"; if (itemFound) { title = itemFound[0].replace('[持有]', '').trim(); '🕵️ 暗標' : '📢 公開比價'; desc = typeLabel + " | 起標價：" + startBid + " " + displayCurrency + " | 點擊立即前往查看詳情並出價！"; if (found[8]) image = found[8].toString().trim(); } var targetUrl = "https://jay870122.github.io/DCGI/?auction=" + auctionId; var html = "" + "" + "" + title + "" + "" + "" + "" + "" + "" + "" + "轉跳至拍賣會中..."; return HtmlService.createHtmlOutput(html); } function jsonResponse(data) { return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify(data)).setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON); } // 🌟🔒 用 Discord OAuth 的 accessToken 向 Discord 官方 API 換回「真正」的使用者ID(絕對不能信任前端自己說自己是誰)。 // 驗證失敗(token無效/過期/被吊銷/沒帶)一律回傳 null,呼叫端要擋掉整個請求。 // 有做短期快取(5分鐘):同一個 token 短時間內重複打 API 不用每次都真的呼叫 Discord,减少延遲跟被 Discord 那邊限流的風險, // 快取用 token 的雜湊值當 key,不會把原始 token 存進快取。 function verifyDiscordToken_(accessToken) { accessToken = (accessToken || '').toString().trim(); if (!accessToken) return null; var cache = CacheService.getScriptCache(); var digest = Utilities.computeDigest(Utilities.DigestAlgorithm.SHA_256, accessToken); var cacheKey = 'dctok_' + Utilities.base64EncodeWebSafe(digest).substring(0, 40); var cached = cache.get(cacheKey); if (cached) return cached; try { var res = UrlFetchApp.fetch('https://discord.com/api/users/@me', { headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + accessToken }, muteHttpExceptions: true, }); if (res.getResponseCode() !== 200) return null; // token 無效/過期,Discord 會回 401 var data = JSON.parse(res.getContentText()); if (!data || !data.id) return null; cache.put(cacheKey, data.id.toString(), 1800); // 🌟 快取30分鐘(原本5分鐘太短,常常要重新跟Discord打招呼,是造成偶發性讀取卡住的主因之一) return data.id.toString(); } catch (e) { return null; } } // 🌟 取得使用者目前的身分組 ID 列表 // 改為直接讀「玩家表」裡 PLAYER_ROLE_COLUMN 那個欄位(由 Skript Bot 主動寫入,逗號分隔多個身分組ID) // 不再呼叫 Discord API,徹底避開 Cloudflare 擋下 GAS/Worker 連線的問題 // 🌟 從玩家表查詢某個DiscordID的Discord顯示名稱(由Skript同步寫入,跟getUserRoles同樣資料來源,可選擇傳入已讀好的playerData共用) function getPlayerDisplayName_(discordId, ss, playerData) { if (!playerData) { ss = ss || SpreadsheetApp.openById(SHEET_ID); var playerSheetForName = ss.getSheets()[0]; playerData = playerSheetForName.getDataRange().getValues(); } var headers = playerData[0]; var colIdx = headers.indexOf(PLAYER_NAME_COLUMN); if (colIdx === -1) return null; for (var i = 1; i < playerData.length; i++) { if (playerData[i][0] && playerData[i][0].toString().replace("'", "") === discordId.toString()) { var raw = playerData[i][colIdx]; return raw ? raw.toString().trim() : null; } } return null; } function getUserRoles(discordId, ss, playerData) { if (!playerData) { ss = ss || SpreadsheetApp.openById(SHEET_ID); var playerSheet = ss.getSheets()[0]; playerData = playerSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); } var headers = playerData[0]; var colIdx = headers.indexOf(PLAYER_ROLE_COLUMN); if (colIdx === -1) return []; // 欄位還沒被建立(Skript Bot 還沒寫過資料) for (var i = 1; i < playerData.length; i++) { if (playerData[i][0].toString().replace("'", "") === discordId.toString()) { var raw = playerData[i][colIdx]; if (!raw) return []; var rawStr = raw.toString().replace("'", ""); // 🌟 去掉寫入時為了強制存文字而加的前置單引號 return rawStr.split(',').map(function(s) { return s.trim(); }).filter(function(s) { return s; }); } } return []; // 找不到此玩家 } // 🌟 取得身分組「ID -> 顯示名稱」對照表 // 改為讀取 ROLE_NAME_MAP_SHEET 這個工作表(管理員手動維護: A欄=身分組ID, B欄=顯示名稱) // 若找不到對照,會直接顯示原始ID,不影響功能運作 function getGuildRoleMap(ss) { ss = ss || SpreadsheetApp.openById(SHEET_ID); var map = {}; var roleMapSheet = ss.getSheetByName(ROLE_NAME_MAP_SHEET); if (roleMapSheet) { var data = roleMapSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) { if (data[i][0] && data[i][1]) { // 🌟 A欄ID跟B欄名稱都要有填,沒填名稱的不算數(避免被當成"已知"身分組) var id = data[i][0].toString().trim(); map[id] = data[i][1].toString().trim(); } } } return map; } // 🌟 檢查使用者身分組是否符合商品要求 (requiredRoleStr 為逗號分隔的身分組ID；空字串=不限；只要符合其中一個即可通過) // 🌟 解析商品的身分組限定設定,支援三種寫法: // "111,222,333" -> 預設:符合其中任一個即可 (向下相容舊格式) // "ANY:111,222,333" -> 跟預設一樣,符合其中任一個即可 // "ALL:111,222,333" -> 必須全部都持有 // "2:111,222,333" -> 至少要持有其中 2 個(數字可換成任意X,代表"其中X個") function parseRoleRequirement(requiredRoleStr) { var result = { mode: 'ANY', minCount: 1, ids: [] }; if (!requiredRoleStr) return result; var raw = requiredRoleStr.toString().trim(); raw = raw.replace(/^'/, ''); // 🌟 防禦性處理:去掉可能殘留的前導單引號(強制文字格式用的標記,理論上讀取時不會出現,保險起見還是清一下) if (!raw) return result; var idsPart = raw; var colonIdx = raw.indexOf(':'); if (colonIdx !== -1) { var prefix = raw.substring(0, colonIdx).trim().toUpperCase(); var afterColon = raw.substring(colonIdx + 1); if (prefix === 'ALL') { result.mode = 'ALL'; idsPart = afterColon; } else if (prefix === 'ANY') { result.mode = 'ANY'; idsPart = afterColon; } else if (/^[0-9]+$/.test(prefix)) { result.mode = 'COUNT'; result.minCount = parseInt(prefix); idsPart = afterColon; } // 辨識不出來的前綴(例如真的是用冒號當分隔符的舊資料)就不拆,整段當作ID清單繼續往下處理 } result.ids = idsPart.split(',').map(function(s) { return s.trim(); }).filter(function(s) { return s; }); return result; } // 🌟 檢查使用者身分組是否符合商品要求 (依照 parseRoleRequirement 解析出的模式判斷:ANY/ALL/COUNT) function checkRolePermission(userRoles, requiredRoleStr) { var req = parseRoleRequirement(requiredRoleStr); if (req.ids.length === 0) return true; if (req.mode === 'ALL') { for (var i = 0; i < req.ids.length; i++) { if (userRoles.indexOf(req.ids[i]) === -1) return false; } return true; } else if (req.mode === 'COUNT') { var matchCount = 0; for (var i = 0; i < req.ids.length; i++) { if (userRoles.indexOf(req.ids[i]) !== -1) matchCount++; } return matchCount >= req.minCount; } else { // ANY for (var i = 0; i < req.ids.length; i++) { if (userRoles.indexOf(req.ids[i]) !== -1) return true; } return false; } } // ============================================================ // 🎰 抽獎模式:身分組加權解析 // ============================================================ // 🌟 解析「身分組ID:倍數,身分組ID:倍數」格式 → {roleId: 倍數} function parseRaffleWeights_(weightStr) { var map = {}; if (!weightStr) return map; weightStr.toString().split(',').forEach(function (pair) { var parts = pair.split(':'); if (parts.length === 2) { var rid = parts[0].trim(), mult = parseFloat(parts[1].trim()); if (rid && mult > 0) map[rid] = mult; } }); return map; } // 🌟 玩家可能同時有多個身分組,取「最高」倍率(不疊加) function getRaffleMultiplier_(userRoles, weightMap) { var best = 1; for (var i = 0; i < userRoles.length; i++) { var m = weightMap[userRoles[i]]; if (m && m > best) best = m; } return best; } function safeParseJSON_(str) { try { return JSON.parse(str); } catch (e) { return null; } } // ============================================================ // 🎲 賭博模式:下注選項解析 // 格式:「選項名稱:賠率,選項名稱:賠率,...」(固定賠率模式用賠率;集資池模式賠率可省略,填不填都不影響計算) // 例如:A隊獲勝:2.0,B隊獲勝:1.8,平手:5.0 或 A隊獲勝,B隊獲勝,平手 // ============================================================ function parseGamblingOptions_(raw) { var result = []; // [{name, odds}] if (!raw) return result; raw.toString().split(',').forEach(function (part) { var seg = part.trim(); if (!seg) return; var ci = seg.indexOf(':'); if (ci !== -1) { var optName = seg.substring(0, ci).trim(); var odds = parseFloat(seg.substring(ci + 1).trim()); if (optName) result.push({ name: optName, odds: (odds > 0 ? odds : 0) }); } else { result.push({ name: seg, odds: 0 }); } }); return result; } // 🌟 商品/分類密碼鎖定:檢查+消耗解鎖密碼(固定密碼或一次性序號皆可),並處理永久解鎖記錄。 // lockType: 'ITEM' 或 'CATEGORY', targetKey: 商品ID或分類名稱(要跟解鎖記錄裡存的值一致,用來辨識這是「哪一個」鎖) // fixedPassword/codeName/persistent: 該商品/分類的鎖定設定(從商店表或分類鎖定設定表讀出來的原始值) // submittedPassword: 玩家這次購買時附上的密碼 // 回傳: // { locked: false } → 這一關不用管(本來就沒設密碼,或已經永久解鎖過) // { locked: true, unlocked: true } → 這次密碼正確,解鎖成功(永久模式的話已經寫入解鎖記錄) // { locked: true, unlocked: false, message: '...' } → 還是鎖著,原因寫在 message // 🌟 依「週期」算出目前這個週期的識別字串(用來跟密碼種子一起雜湊出當期密碼) // DAILY=當天日期(依試算表所在時區,例如台北時區的午夜為分界), WEEKLY=ISO週次, MONTHLY=當月 function getPeriodKey_(mode) { var tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone() || 'Asia/Taipei'; var now = new Date(); mode = (mode || '').toString().trim().toUpperCase(); if (mode === 'MONTHLY') return Utilities.formatDate(now, tz, 'yyyy-MM'); if (mode === 'WEEKLY') { // ISO 8601 週次算法 var d = new Date(Utilities.formatDate(now, tz, "yyyy/MM/dd")); var day = (d.getDay() + 6) % 7; // 週一=0 d.setDate(d.getDate() - day + 3); // 移到這週的週四 var firstThursday = new Date(d.getFullYear(), 0, 4); var week = 1 + Math.round(((d - firstThursday) / 86400000 - 3 + ((firstThursday.getDay() + 6) % 7)) / 7); return d.getFullYear() + '-W' + (week < 10 ? '0' + week : week); } return Utilities.formatDate(now, tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd'); // DAILY(預設) } // 🌟 用「密碼種子」+「目前週期」雜湊出這個週期的密碼(6碼英數字,全大寫,同一週期內固定不變,週期一到就自動換一組) function computeRotatingPassword_(mode, seed) { seed = (seed || '').toString().trim(); if (!seed) return ''; var periodKey = getPeriodKey_(mode); var raw = Utilities.computeDigest(Utilities.DigestAlgorithm.SHA_256, seed + '|' + periodKey); var hex = raw.map(function(b) { var v = (b < 0 ? b + 256 : b).toString(16); return v.length < 2 ? '0' + v : v; }).join(''); return hex.substring(0, 6).toUpperCase(); } // 🌟 給管理後台看的「這個週期是哪一期」的人話說明 function describePeriod_(mode) { mode = (mode || '').toString().trim().toUpperCase(); var key = getPeriodKey_(mode); if (mode === 'MONTHLY') return '本月(' + key + ')'; if (mode === 'WEEKLY') return '本週(' + key + ')'; return '今天(' + key + ')'; } // 🌟 從「自訂密碼表」文字裡找出某個週期代碼對應的密碼 // 格式:一行一組,「週期代碼=密碼」或「週期代碼:密碼」都可以,例如 2026-07-03=ABC123 function lookupSchedulePassword_(scheduleText, periodKey) { var lines = (scheduleText || '').toString().split(/\r?\n/); for (var i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) { var line = lines[i].trim(); if (!line) continue; var idx = line.indexOf('='); if (idx === -1) idx = line.indexOf(':'); if (idx === -1) continue; var key = line.substring(0, idx).trim(); var pw = line.substring(idx + 1).trim(); if (key === periodKey && pw) return pw; } return ''; // 這期沒有排到密碼 } // 🌟 算出「目前這個週期」應該比對的密碼:優先看「自訂密碼表」裡有沒有排這一期, // 有排就直接用管理員自己填的密碼；沒排到(或整個沒用自訂密碼表)才退回用「密碼種子」自動雜湊產生 function getExpectedRotatingPassword_(mode, seed, schedule) { if (schedule && schedule.toString().trim()) { return lookupSchedulePassword_(schedule, getPeriodKey_(mode)); // 找不到就回傳空字串 = 這期用這個方式解不開,要管理員去補 } return computeRotatingPassword_(mode, seed); } // 🌟 查今天這個人對這個鎖(商品/分類)已經猜錯過幾次 function getAttemptCount_(ss, discordId, lockType, targetKey, dateKey) { var sheet = ss.getSheetByName(PASSWORD_ATTEMPT_SHEET_NAME); if (!sheet) return 0; var data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues(); for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) { if (data[i][0] && data[i][0].toString().replace("'", "").trim() === dateKey && data[i][1] && data[i][1].toString().replace("'", "") === discordId.toString() && data[i][2] === lockType && data[i][3] && data[i][3].toString() === targetKey.toString()) { return parseInt(data[i][4], 10) || 0; } } return 0; } // 🌟 猜錯一次,把今天這個人對這個鎖的嘗試次數 +1(第一次猜錯會自動建立這張工作表跟這一列) function incrementAttemptCount_(ss, discordId, lockType, targetKey, dateKey) { var sheet = ss.getSheetByName(PASSWORD_ATTEMPT_SHEET_NAME); if (!sheet) { sheet = ss.insertSheet(PASSWORD_ATTEMPT_SHEET_NAME); sheet.appendRow(['日期', 'DiscordID', '類型(ITEM/CATEGORY)', '對象', '今日嘗試次數']); } var data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues(); for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) { if (data[i][0] && data[i][0].toString().replace("'", "").trim() === dateKey && data[i][1] && data[i][1].toString().replace("'", "") === discordId.toString() && data[i][2] === lockType && data[i][3] && data[i][3].toString() === targetKey.toString()) { var newCount = (parseInt(data[i][4], 10) || 0) + 1; sheet.getRange(i + 1, 5).setValue(newCount); return newCount; } } sheet.appendRow(["'" + dateKey, "'" + discordId.toString(), lockType, targetKey.toString(), 1]); return 1; } // 🌟 通用的密碼鎖定驗證(商品/分類共用): // fixedPassword(固定密碼)、codeName(一次性序號)、passwordMode+(passwordSeed自動產生 或 passwordSchedule自訂密碼表)三種方式擇一成功即可解鎖 // guessLimitEnabled+guessLimitCount+guessLimitPeriod:開啟後,同一個人在同一期(每日/每週/每月,可選)內對同一個鎖最多只能猜 N 次(猜對不算,只算猜錯),超過要等下一期 function checkUnlock_(ss, discordId, lockType, targetKey, fixedPassword, codeName, persistent, submittedPassword, passwordMode, passwordSeed, passwordSchedule, guessLimitEnabled, guessLimitCount, guessLimitPeriod) { fixedPassword = (fixedPassword || '').toString().trim(); codeName = (codeName || '').toString().trim(); passwordMode = (passwordMode || '').toString().trim().toUpperCase(); passwordSeed = (passwordSeed || '').toString().trim(); passwordSchedule = (passwordSchedule || '').toString(); guessLimitEnabled = (guessLimitEnabled === true) || (guessLimitEnabled && guessLimitEnabled.toString().trim().toUpperCase() === 'Y'); guessLimitCount = parseInt(guessLimitCount, 10) || 0; guessLimitPeriod = (guessLimitPeriod || 'DAILY').toString().trim().toUpperCase(); if (['DAILY', 'WEEKLY', 'MONTHLY'].indexOf(guessLimitPeriod) === -1) guessLimitPeriod = 'DAILY'; var hasRotating = !!(passwordMode && (passwordSeed || passwordSchedule.trim())); if (!fixedPassword && !codeName && !hasRotating) return { locked: false }; // 沒設定任何一種密碼,不用鎖 var isPersistent = (persistent || '').toString().trim().toUpperCase() !== 'SESSION'; // 留空預設「永久解鎖」,填 SESSION 才是每次都要重新輸入 if (isPersistent) { var logSheet = ss.getSheetByName(UNLOCK_LOG_SHEET_NAME); if (logSheet) { var logData = logSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); // A時間 | B DiscordID | C 類型(ITEM/CATEGORY) | D 對象(商品ID或分類名稱) for (var i = 1; i < logData.length; i++) { if (logData[i][1] && logData[i][1].toString().replace("'", "") === discordId.toString() && logData[i][2] === lockType && logData[i][3] && logData[i][3].toString() === targetKey.toString()) { return { locked: false }; // 之前已經永久解鎖過,這次不用再檢查密碼 } } } } submittedPassword = (submittedPassword || '').toString().trim(); if (!submittedPassword) { return { locked: true, unlocked: false, message: (lockType === 'CATEGORY' ? '此分類的商品' : '此商品') + '需要密碼才能購買,請輸入密碼' }; } // 🌟 猜測次數上限(每日/每週/每月可選):先檢查這一期是不是已經用完額度,用完的話直接擋掉,不用再比對密碼(也不會多算一次) var limitPeriodLabel = { DAILY: '今天', WEEKLY: '這一週', MONTHLY: '這個月' }[guessLimitPeriod]; var limitPeriodKey = 'GUESS-' + guessLimitPeriod + '-' + getPeriodKey_(guessLimitPeriod); // 加前綴避免跟其他用途的期別代碼混在同一張記錄表裡搞混 var attemptsSoFar = 0; if (guessLimitEnabled && guessLimitCount > 0) { attemptsSoFar = getAttemptCount_(ss, discordId, lockType, targetKey, limitPeriodKey); if (attemptsSoFar >= guessLimitCount) { return { locked: true, unlocked: false, message: limitPeriodLabel + '嘗試密碼的次數已經用完了(上限 ' + guessLimitCount + ' 次),請等下一期再試' }; } } var success = false; var expectedRotatingPw = hasRotating ? getExpectedRotatingPassword_(passwordMode, passwordSeed, passwordSchedule) : ''; if (fixedPassword && submittedPassword === fixedPassword) { success = true; } else if (expectedRotatingPw && submittedPassword.toUpperCase() === expectedRotatingPw.toUpperCase()) { success = true; // 🌟 自動輪替密碼(自訂密碼表優先,沒排到才用種子自動產生；每日/每週/每月變一次,不分大小寫比對) } else if (codeName) { var unlockKeySheet = ss.getSheetByName(UNLOCK_KEY_SHEET_NAME); if (unlockKeySheet) { var keyData = unlockKeySheet.getDataRange().getValues(); // A名稱(對應設定裡的codeName) | B序號/密碼 | C狀態(留空=可用,填了就是已使用) | D使用者DiscordID(系統寫入) for (var k = 1; k < keyData.length; k++) { if (keyData[k][0] && keyData[k][0].toString().trim() === codeName && keyData[k][1] && keyData[k][1].toString().trim() === submittedPassword && (!keyData[k][2] || keyData[k][2].toString().trim() === '')) { unlockKeySheet.getRange(k + 1, 3).setValue('已使用'); unlockKeySheet.getRange(k + 1, 4).setValue("'" + discordId.toString()); success = true; break; } } } } if (!success) { var remainMsg = ''; if (guessLimitEnabled && guessLimitCount > 0) { var newCount = incrementAttemptCount_(ss, discordId, lockType, targetKey, limitPeriodKey); var remain = Math.max(0, guessLimitCount - newCount); remainMsg = remain > 0 ? ('(' + limitPeriodLabel + '還可以再猜 ' + remain + ' 次)') : ('(' + limitPeriodLabel + '的嘗試次數已經用完了,請等下一期再試)'); } return { locked: true, unlocked: false, message: '密碼錯誤,或序號已經被使用過' + remainMsg }; } if (isPersistent) { var logSheet2 = ss.getSheetByName(UNLOCK_LOG_SHEET_NAME); if (logSheet2) logSheet2.appendRow([new Date(), "'" + discordId.toString(), lockType, targetKey.toString()]); } return { locked: true, unlocked: true }; } // 🌟 找出某個分類的鎖定設定(固定密碼/一次性序號名稱/持續性),沒設定過就回傳全空物件 function getCategoryLockConfig_(ss, categoryName) { var sheet = ss.getSheetByName(CATEGORY_LOCK_SHEET_NAME); if (!sheet || !categoryName) return { fixedPassword: '', codeName: '', persistent: '', visibility: '', showHint: '', hintText: '', passwordMode: '', passwordSeed: '', passwordSchedule: '', guessLimitEnabled: '', guessLimitCount: 0, guessLimitPeriod: 'DAILY' }; var data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues(); for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) { if (data[i][0] && data[i][0].toString().trim() === categoryName.toString().trim()) { return { fixedPassword: data[i][1] ? data[i][1].toString() : '', codeName: data[i][2] ? data[i][2].toString() : '', persistent: data[i][3] ? data[i][3].toString() : '', visibility: data[i][4] ? data[i][4].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : '', // E(4) 留空/HIDDEN=解鎖前完全不顯示內容, BLUR=解鎖前顯示模糊預覽, VISIBLE=正常顯示只鎖購買 showHint: data[i][5] ? data[i][5].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : '', // F(5) 只在「完全隱藏」模式下才有意義:留空/SHOW=側邊欄照常顯示這個分類(帶🔒圖示), HIDE=側邊欄完全不列出這個分類 hintText: data[i][6] ? data[i][6].toString() : '', // G(6) 密碼提示詞(只在「正常顯示」/「模糊顯示」模式下會顯示給玩家看) passwordMode: data[i][7] ? data[i][7].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : '', // H(7) 🌟 自動輪替密碼週期(留空=不啟用/DAILY/WEEKLY/MONTHLY) passwordSeed: data[i][8] ? data[i][8].toString() : '', // I(8) 🌟 自動輪替密碼種子 passwordSchedule: data[i][9] ? data[i][9].toString() : '', // J(9) 🌟 自訂密碼表(有排的期別優先於種子自動產生) guessLimitEnabled: data[i][10] ? data[i][10].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : '', // K(10) 🌟 是否開啟猜測次數上限(Y=開啟) guessLimitCount: data[i][11] ? parseInt(data[i][11], 10) || 0 : 0, // L(11) 🌟 每期最多可猜幾次 guessLimitPeriod: data[i][12] ? data[i][12].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : 'DAILY', // M(12) 🌟 次數上限重置週期(留空=每日/DAILY/WEEKLY/MONTHLY) }; } } return { fixedPassword: '', codeName: '', persistent: '', visibility: '', showHint: '', hintText: '', passwordMode: '', passwordSeed: '', passwordSchedule: '', guessLimitEnabled: '', guessLimitCount: 0, guessLimitPeriod: 'DAILY' }; } // 🌟 獨立驗證「分類」密碼(不透過購買商品):玩家點選被鎖定的分類時,要先解鎖才能看到裡面的商品內容 function unlockCategory(discordId, category, unlockPassword) { var lock = LockService.getScriptLock(); lock.waitLock(10000); try { var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SHEET_ID); category = (category || '').toString().trim(); if (!category) return { "status": "error", "message": "缺少分類名稱" }; var cfg = getCategoryLockConfig_(ss, category); var result = checkUnlock_(ss, discordId, 'CATEGORY', category, cfg.fixedPassword, cfg.codeName, cfg.persistent, unlockPassword, cfg.passwordMode, cfg.passwordSeed, cfg.passwordSchedule, cfg.guessLimitEnabled, cfg.guessLimitCount, cfg.guessLimitPeriod); if (!result.locked || result.unlocked) { var isPersistent = (cfg.persistent || '').toString().trim().toUpperCase() !== 'SESSION'; return { "status": "success", "message": "解鎖成功", "persistent": isPersistent }; } return { "status": "error", "message": result.message }; } finally { lock.releaseLock(); } } // 🌟 獨立驗證「商品」密碼(不透過購買):模糊顯示模式的商品要先解鎖才能看到完整內容 function unlockItem(discordId, itemId, unlockPassword) { var lock = LockService.getScriptLock(); lock.waitLock(10000); try { var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SHEET_ID); var shopSheet = ss.getSheets()[1]; var shopData = shopSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); itemId = (itemId || '').toString().trim(); if (!itemId) return { "status": "error", "message": "缺少商品ID" }; var shopRowIndex = -1; for (var i = 1; i < shopData.length; i++) { if (shopData[i][18] && shopData[i][18].toString().trim() === itemId) { shopRowIndex = i; break; } } if (shopRowIndex === -1) return { "status": "error", "message": "找不到該商品" }; var fixedPassword = shopData[shopRowIndex][25] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][25].toString() : ''; var codeName = shopData[shopRowIndex][26] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][26].toString() : ''; var persistent = shopData[shopRowIndex][27] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][27].toString() : ''; var passwordMode = shopData[shopRowIndex][30] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][30].toString() : ''; // AE(30) 🌟 自動輪替密碼週期 var passwordSeed = shopData[shopRowIndex][31] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][31].toString() : ''; // AF(31) 🌟 自動輪替密碼種子 var passwordSchedule = shopData[shopRowIndex][32] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][32].toString() : ''; // AG(32) 🌟 自訂密碼表 var guessLimitEnabled = shopData[shopRowIndex][33] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][33].toString() : ''; // AH(33) 🌟 是否開啟猜測次數上限 var guessLimitCount = shopData[shopRowIndex][34] ? parseInt(shopData[shopRowIndex][34], 10) || 0 : 0; // AI(34) 🌟 每期最多可猜幾次 var guessLimitPeriod = shopData[shopRowIndex][35] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][35].toString() : 'DAILY'; // AJ(35) 🌟 次數上限重置週期 var result = checkUnlock_(ss, discordId, 'ITEM', itemId, fixedPassword, codeName, persistent, unlockPassword, passwordMode, passwordSeed, passwordSchedule, guessLimitEnabled, guessLimitCount, guessLimitPeriod); if (!result.locked || result.unlocked) { var isPersistent = (persistent || '').toString().trim().toUpperCase() !== 'SESSION'; return { "status": "success", "message": "解鎖成功", "persistent": isPersistent }; } return { "status": "error", "message": result.message }; } finally { lock.releaseLock(); } } // 🌟 除錯用：在 Apps Script 編輯器選這個函式按「執行」，到「執行紀錄/記錄」(Logger) 看設定狀況 // 把下面 TEST_DISCORD_ID 換成你自己的 Discord ID 再執行，用完可以刪掉，不影響正式功能 function debugCheckRoleSetup() { var TEST_DISCORD_ID = '176681551189377024'; // 🌟 換成你要測試的 Discord ID var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SHEET_ID); var playerSheet = ss.getSheets()[0]; var headers = playerSheet.getDataRange().getValues()[0]; var colIdx = headers.indexOf(PLAYER_ROLE_COLUMN); Logger.log('玩家表是否已有「' + PLAYER_ROLE_COLUMN + '」欄位: ' + (colIdx !== -1 ? '有 (第' + (colIdx + 1) + '欄)' : '沒有(Skript Bot 還沒寫過資料,或欄位名稱對不上)')); var roleMapSheet = ss.getSheetByName(ROLE_NAME_MAP_SHEET); Logger.log('是否已建立「' + ROLE_NAME_MAP_SHEET + '」工作表: ' + (roleMapSheet ? '有' : '沒有(會直接顯示身分組原始ID,不影響功能)')); var roles = getUserRoles(TEST_DISCORD_ID); Logger.log('測試 Discord ID [' + TEST_DISCORD_ID + '] 目前讀到的身分組: ' + (roles.length > 0 ? roles.join(', ') : '(空)')); var roleMap = getGuildRoleMap(); Logger.log('身分組對照表內容: ' + JSON.stringify(roleMap)); } function parseGachaRules(rawText) { var lines = rawText.toString().split("\n"), pool = []; for (var i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) { var line = lines[i].trim(); if (!line) continue; var parts = line.split(",").map(function(s) { return s.trim(); }); var dispName = parts[0]; var varList = null; // 🌟 多變數格式:[{varName, qty}, ...],一個獎項同時發放好幾種貨幣/道具 var singleVarName = dispName, singleQty = 1; // 🌟 單一變數格式用(相容舊寫法) var prob = null, stock = null; for (var p = 1; p < parts.length; p++) { var token = parts[p]; if (token === "") continue; if (token.indexOf('%') !== -1) { prob = parseFloat(token.replace('%','')); continue; } if (token.indexOf('份') !== -1 || token.indexOf('個') !== -1) { stock = parseInt(token.replace(/[^0-9-]/g, '')); continue; } if (!isNaN(token) && !isNaN(parseFloat(token))) { singleQty = parseInt(token); continue; } // 🌟 剩下的文字token:含「+」= 多變數(粽子:1+黃金粽:1),不含則是單一變數名(可選:數量,例如 粽子:5) if (token.indexOf('+') !== -1) { varList = token.split('+').map(function(seg) { seg = seg.trim(); var colonIdx = seg.indexOf(':'); if (colonIdx !== -1) { return { varName: seg.substring(0, colonIdx).trim(), qty: parseInt(seg.substring(colonIdx + 1)) || 1 }; } return { varName: seg, qty: 1 }; }); } else { var colonIdx2 = token.indexOf(':'); if (colonIdx2 !== -1) { singleVarName = token.substring(0, colonIdx2).trim(); singleQty = parseInt(token.substring(colonIdx2 + 1)) || 1; } else { singleVarName = token; } } } if (!varList) varList = [{ varName: singleVarName, qty: singleQty }]; // 🌟 varName/qty 保留第一個變數,給還沒改寫的舊程式碼/前端相容用;varList 是完整清單,真正發獎要用這個 pool.push({ dispName: dispName, varList: varList, varName: varList[0].varName, qty: varList[0].qty, prob: prob, stock: stock }); } return pool; } // 🌟 從一個盲盒獎池抽一次獎(機率→有庫存的按庫存比例均分抽樣→保底),邏輯跟商品本身的盲盒抽獎完全一樣。 // 中獎的話會把該獎項的 .stock 在「傳進來的這個池子」裡扣1(只影響呼叫端傳進來的這份拷貝,不會自動寫回試算表)。 // 回傳中獎的獎項物件({dispName, varList, ...}),或 null(池子是空的、或機率沒中也沒有庫存/保底可以撿) function drawOneFromGachaPool_(pool) { if (!pool || pool.length === 0) return null; var wonItem = null, roll = Math.random() * 100, cumulative = 0; for (var i = 0; i < pool.length; i++) { var p = pool[i]; if (p.prob !== null) { cumulative += p.prob; if (roll <= cumulative) { if (p.stock === null || p.stock > 0) wonItem = p; break; } } } if (!wonItem) { var totalStock = 0, kujiPool = []; for (var i = 0; i < pool.length; i++) { if (pool[i].prob === null && pool[i].stock !== null && pool[i].stock > 0) { totalStock += pool[i].stock; kujiPool.push(pool[i]); } } if (totalStock > 0) { var kRoll = Math.random() * totalStock, kCum = 0; for (var i = 0; i < kujiPool.length; i++) { kCum += kujiPool[i].stock; if (kRoll <= kCum) { wonItem = kujiPool[i]; break; } } } } if (!wonItem) { var fallbacks = []; for (var i = 0; i < pool.length; i++) { if (pool[i].prob === null && pool[i].stock === null) fallbacks.push(pool[i]); } if (fallbacks.length > 0) wonItem = fallbacks[Math.floor(Math.random() * fallbacks.length)]; } if (wonItem && wonItem.stock !== null) wonItem.stock -= 1; return wonItem; } // 🌟 累積兌換次數里程碑獎勵:一行一個里程碑,格式「達成累積兌換數量 => 獎勵」 // 獎勵語法沿用盲盒規則的變數寫法:可以用「+」串連同時發多種(例如 水晶:100+序號:1),也支援 [序號]/[非即時] 前綴 // 例如: // 10 => 水晶:100 // 20 => 水晶:300,道具:1 ← 注意這裡改用「+」不是逗號,逗號在這個語法裡沒有特殊意義,只是方便閱讀 // 回傳依累積數量由小到大排序過的 [{count, varList:[{varName,qty}]}] // 🌟 里程碑規則格式:「次數 => 獎勵」是一次性的(只有累積剛好到那個數字時發一次); // 「每N => 獎勵」是重複性的(累積每滿N的倍數就會再發一次,例如「每5」在第5、10、15、20...次都會發)。 // 兩種可以混用、可以同時設好幾條。 // 如果想要有一個好看的顯示名稱(而不是直接顯示變數名),可以在獎勵前面加「顯示名稱 | 」,例如: // 10 => 水晶寶箱 | 水晶:100 // 🌟 也可以加庫存(限量,發完就沒有了,格式跟盲盒一樣用「, N份」加在最後面),例如: // 每5 => 水晶寶箱 | 水晶:20, 50份 ← 這個「每5」的獎勵總共只有50份可以發,發完之後里程碑到了也不會再送 // 🌟🎁 也可以做成「盲盒式」里程碑:達到這個里程碑時不是固定發一種獎勵,而是像抽獎一樣從一個獎池裡隨機抽一個。 // 寫法:「數量 =>」後面不接任何東西(留空),接下來幾行(直到下一個「數量 =>」開頭的行為止)就是這個里程碑的獎池, // 語法跟商品本身的「盲盒規則」完全一樣(顯示名稱, 變數:數量, 機率%, 庫存),例如: // 10 => // 水晶寶箱, 水晶:100, 60% // 傳說寶箱, [序號]傳說道具:1, 10%, 5份 // 安慰獎, 水晶:10 // // 每5 => 水晶:20 function parseMilestoneRules(rawText) { var lines = (rawText || '').toString().split('\n'); var milestones = []; var headerPattern = /^(每)?\d+\s*=>/; var i = 0; while (i < lines.length) { var line = lines[i].trim(); i++; if (!line) continue; var arrowIdx = line.indexOf('=>'); if (arrowIdx === -1) continue; var countPart = line.substring(0, arrowIdx).trim(); var rewardPart = line.substring(arrowIdx + 2).trim(); var repeat = false; if (countPart.charAt(0) === '每') { repeat = true; countPart = countPart.substring(1).trim(); } var count = parseInt(countPart, 10); if (!count || count <= 0) continue; if (rewardPart === '') { // 🌟 盲盒式里程碑:收集接下來的行當作獎池,直到遇到下一個里程碑標頭行或文字結束為止 var poolLines = []; while (i < lines.length) { var peek = lines[i].trim(); if (headerPattern.test(peek)) break; if (peek !== '') poolLines.push(peek); i++; } var pool = parseGachaRules(poolLines.join('\n')); if (pool.length > 0) milestones.push({ count: count, repeat: repeat, isGacha: true, gachaPool: pool }); continue; } // 🌟 先抓尾端的庫存(例如「, 50份」或「, 50個」),要在拆解顯示名稱/獎勵之前先抓,避免庫存數字被誤判成獎勵的一部分 var stock = null; var stockMatch = rewardPart.match(/,\s*(\d+)\s*[份個]\s*$/); if (stockMatch) { stock = parseInt(stockMatch[1], 10); rewardPart = rewardPart.substring(0, stockMatch.index).trim(); } // 🌟 可選的顯示名稱:「顯示名稱 | 變數:數量+變數:數量」,沒有「|」的話就直接顯示變數內容本身 var displayName = null, actualRewardPart = rewardPart; var pipeIdx = rewardPart.indexOf('|'); if (pipeIdx !== -1) { displayName = rewardPart.substring(0, pipeIdx).trim(); actualRewardPart = rewardPart.substring(pipeIdx + 1).trim(); } var varList = actualRewardPart.split('+').map(function(seg) { seg = seg.trim(); var colonIdx = seg.indexOf(':'); if (colonIdx !== -1) return { varName: seg.substring(0, colonIdx).trim(), qty: parseInt(seg.substring(colonIdx + 1), 10) || 1 }; return { varName: seg, qty: 1 }; }).filter(function(v) { return v.varName; }); if (varList.length > 0) milestones.push({ count: count, repeat: repeat, isGacha: false, varList: varList, displayName: displayName, rewardText: displayName || actualRewardPart, stock: stock }); } milestones.sort(function(a, b) { return a.count - b.count; }); return milestones; } // 🌟 把 parseMilestoneRules 解析出來的規則(可能已經扣過庫存)重新組回原本的文字格式,寫回試算表用 // (寫回時只會把「原本就有標庫存」的規則的庫存數字更新,格式跟解析時完全對稱;盲盒式里程碑的獎池庫存也會一併寫回) function serializeMilestoneRules(milestones) { var lines = []; for (var i = 0; i < milestones.length; i++) { var m = milestones[i]; var countPart = (m.repeat ? '每' : '') + m.count; if (m.isGacha) { lines.push(countPart + ' =>'); m.gachaPool.forEach(function(p) { var seg = p.dispName + ', ' + p.varList.map(function(v) { return v.varName + ':' + v.qty; }).join('+'); if (p.prob !== null) seg += ', ' + p.prob + '%'; if (p.stock !== null) seg += ', ' + p.stock + '份'; lines.push(seg); }); } else { var rewardSpec = m.varList.map(function(v) { return v.varName + ':' + v.qty; }).join('+'); var rewardPart = m.displayName ? (m.displayName + ' | ' + rewardSpec) : rewardSpec; if (m.stock !== null && m.stock !== undefined) rewardPart += ', ' + m.stock + '份'; lines.push(countPart + ' => ' + rewardPart); } } return lines.join('\n'); } // 🌟 把一組 varList(例如 [{varName:'水晶',qty:100}, {varName:'[序號]傳說道具',qty:1}])實際發放給玩家。 // 跟盲盒中獎後的發放邏輯共用同一套規則([序號]查序號庫、幻彩水晶同步升階1/2、[非即時]不自動入帳)。 // 回傳 {resultStrs} 成功;或 {error} 失敗(呼叫端要讓整筆購買失敗,不能只發一半) function grantVarListToPlayer_(varList, playerHeaders, playerData, playerRow, playerSheet, keySheet, keyData, discordId, assignedKeys) { var resultStrs = []; for (var wv = 0; wv < varList.length; wv++) { var vKey = varList[wv].varName; var amt = varList[wv].qty; if (vKey.indexOf("[序號]") !== -1) { if (!keySheet) return { error: "里程碑獎勵抽中序號,但尚未建立「序號庫」工作表！" }; var cleanKeyName = vKey.replace(/\[.*?\]/g, '').trim(); var foundKeysCount = 0; for (var k = 1; k < keyData.length; k++) { var rowKeyName = keyData[k][0] ? keyData[k][0].toString().trim() : ""; if (rowKeyName === cleanKeyName && (keyData[k][2] === "" || keyData[k][2] === null || keyData[k][2] === undefined)) { var keyVal = keySheet.getRange(k + 1, 2).getValue(); assignedKeys.push(keyVal); keySheet.getRange(k + 1, 3).setValue(discordId.toString()); keyData[k][2] = discordId.toString(); foundKeysCount++; if (foundKeysCount >= amt) break; } } if (foundKeysCount < amt) return { error: "里程碑獎勵【" + cleanKeyName + "】序號庫存不足！請聯絡管理員補充。" }; resultStrs.push(vKey + " " + amt); continue; } var isNonInstant = vKey.indexOf("[非即時]") !== -1; var isRoleGrant = vKey.indexOf("[身分組]") !== -1; // 🌟 這是給 Discord 端動態發身分組用的標籤,不是真正的貨幣/道具,不能寫進玩家試算表欄位 if (!isNonInstant && !isRoleGrant) { if (vKey === '幻彩水晶') { var s1ColIdx = playerHeaders.indexOf('升階1'); if (s1ColIdx === -1) { s1ColIdx = playerHeaders.length; playerHeaders.push('升階1'); playerSheet.getRange(1, s1ColIdx + 1).setValue('升階1'); } var s1Bal = parseInt(playerData[playerRow - 1][s1ColIdx]) || 0; playerSheet.getRange(playerRow, s1ColIdx + 1).setValue(s1Bal + amt); playerData[playerRow - 1][s1ColIdx] = s1Bal + amt; var s2ColIdx = playerHeaders.indexOf('升階2'); if (s2ColIdx === -1) { s2ColIdx = playerHeaders.length; playerHeaders.push('升階2'); playerSheet.getRange(1, s2ColIdx + 1).setValue('升階2'); } var s2Bal = parseInt(playerData[playerRow - 1][s2ColIdx]) || 0; playerSheet.getRange(playerRow, s2ColIdx + 1).setValue(s2Bal + amt); playerData[playerRow - 1][s2ColIdx] = s2Bal + amt; } else if (vKey === '可用幻彩水晶') { var s2ColIdx2 = playerHeaders.indexOf('升階2'); if (s2ColIdx2 === -1) { s2ColIdx2 = playerHeaders.length; playerHeaders.push('升階2'); playerSheet.getRange(1, s2ColIdx2 + 1).setValue('升階2'); } var s2Bal2 = parseInt(playerData[playerRow - 1][s2ColIdx2]) || 0; playerSheet.getRange(playerRow, s2ColIdx2 + 1).setValue(s2Bal2 + amt); playerData[playerRow - 1][s2ColIdx2] = s2Bal2 + amt; } else { var colIdx = playerHeaders.indexOf(vKey); if (colIdx === -1) { colIdx = playerHeaders.length; playerHeaders.push(vKey); playerSheet.getRange(1, colIdx + 1).setValue(vKey); } var curBal = parseInt(playerData[playerRow - 1][colIdx]) || 0; playerSheet.getRange(playerRow, colIdx + 1).setValue(curBal + amt); playerData[playerRow - 1][colIdx] = curBal + amt; } } resultStrs.push(vKey + " " + amt); } return { resultStrs: resultStrs }; } // 🌟🔧 共用函式:從指定的「序號庫」名稱依序發一組序號給每個玩家(找不到序號的人會列在failed裡,不會中斷其他人)。 // 這個函式一定會:1) 寫歷史紀錄 2) 排一則 [序號私訊批次] 訊息給瓜.sk,讓瓜「一定」私訊每個人自己拿到的序號 // ——序號不管貨幣調整的「通知」有沒有勾選都一定要私訊,不然等於白發,玩家根本不知道自己中了什麼。 // keyName: 序號庫A欄的對應名稱 | playerIds: 要發放的玩家ID陣列 | itemLabel: 私訊裡顯示的項目說明文字(例如商品名稱) // historyReasonPrefix: 歷史紀錄裡商品名稱欄要顯示的前綴,例如 "[序號發放] " 或 "[拍賣安慰獎] " // 回傳 { granted: {discordId: 序號值}, failed: [discordId,...] } function dispatchSerialCodesToPlayers_(ss, historySheet, keyName, playerIds, itemLabel, historyReasonPrefix) { var result = { granted: {}, failed: [] }; if (!keyName || !playerIds || !playerIds.length) return result; if (ss.getSheets().length < 5) { playerIds.forEach(function (pid) { result.failed.push(pid); }); return result; } var keySheet = ss.getSheets()[4]; var keyData = keySheet.getDataRange().getValues(); var safeItemLabel = (itemLabel || '').toString().replace(/[|,:;=@%]/g, '、'); playerIds.forEach(function (pid) { pid = pid.toString(); var found = false; for (var k = 1; k < keyData.length; k++) { var rowKeyName = keyData[k][0] ? keyData[k][0].toString().trim() : ''; var usedBy = keyData[k][2]; if (rowKeyName === keyName && (usedBy === '' || usedBy === null || usedBy === undefined)) { var keyVal = keySheet.getRange(k + 1, 2).getValue(); keySheet.getRange(k + 1, 3).setValue("'" + pid); keyData[k][2] = pid; // 🌟 更新記憶體副本,避免同一批次裡不同玩家重複發到同一組序號 result.granted[pid] = keyVal; found = true; if (historySheet) { historySheet.appendRow([new Date(), pid, (historyReasonPrefix || "[序號發放] ") + keyName, 1, "", "", "🎫 序號：" + keyVal, "", ""]); } break; } } if (!found) result.failed.push(pid); }); var grantedIds = Object.keys(result.granted); if (grantedIds.length > 0) { // 🌟 整批合併成一則,單層迴圈給瓜.sk處理,不會一人洗一則 var entries = grantedIds.map(function (pid) { return pid + '@' + result.granted[pid].toString().replace(/[|,:;=@%]/g, '、'); }); var skMsg = "[序號私訊批次] " + safeItemLabel + "|" + entries.join(';'); try { queueWebhook_(skMsg); } catch (e) {} } return result; } function serializeGachaRules(pool) { var lines = []; for (var i = 0; i < pool.length; i++) { var p = pool[i]; var parts = [p.dispName]; var varList = (p.varList && p.varList.length > 0) ? p.varList : [{ varName: p.varName, qty: p.qty }]; if (varList.length > 1) { // 🌟 多變數:序列化回 name:qty+name:qty 的格式 parts.push(varList.map(function(v) { return v.varName + ':' + v.qty; }).join('+')); } else { if (varList[0].varName !== p.dispName) parts.push(varList[0].varName); parts.push(varList[0].qty); } if (p.prob !== null) parts.push(p.prob + "%"); if (p.stock !== null) parts.push(p.stock + "份"); lines.push(parts.join(", ")); } return lines.join("\n"); } function getUserHistory(discordId, page, pageSize) { page = parseInt(page) || 1; pageSize = parseInt(pageSize) || 10; if (page < 1) page = 1; if (pageSize < 1) pageSize = 10; if (pageSize > 50) pageSize = 50; // 防呆,避免單次抓太多 var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SHEET_ID); var historySheet = ss.getSheets()[2], data = historySheet.getDataRange().getValues(), matched = []; // 🌟 多抓 1 筆只是用來判斷「還有沒有下一頁」,抓到這個數量就直接停止掃描, // 不用每次都把整張歷史紀錄表從頭掃到尾,使用者紀錄越新越快抓到 var needed = page * pageSize + 1; for (var i = data.length - 1; i >= 1 && matched.length < needed; i--) { if (!data[i][0] || !data[i][1]) continue; if (data[i][1].toString().replace("'", "") === discordId.toString()) { var timeStr = ""; try { timeStr = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(data[i][0]), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "yyyy/MM/dd HH:mm:ss"); } catch(e) { timeStr = "時間讀取錯誤"; } matched.push({ time: timeStr, itemName: data[i][2], qty: data[i][3], keys: data[i][5] || "無", drawn: data[i][6] || "", beforeBal: data[i][7] !== "" ? data[i][7] : null, afterBal: data[i][8] !== "" ? data[i][8] : null, altCost: data[i][9] || "", // 🌟 替代貨幣扣款明細 extraCost: data[i][10] || "", // 🌟 額外必付費用扣款明細 totalRewards: data[i][11] || "" // 🌟 總共獲得的所有變數(已加總) }); } } var hasMore = matched.length > page * pageSize; var startIdx = (page - 1) * pageSize; var pageItems = matched.slice(startIdx, startIdx + pageSize); return { "status": "success", "history": pageItems, "page": page, "pageSize": pageSize, "hasMore": hasMore }; } function getUserScores(discordId, ss, userRoles, roleMap, playerData) { ss = ss || SpreadsheetApp.openById(SHEET_ID); if (!playerData) { var playerSheet = ss.getSheets()[0]; playerData = playerSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); } var s1 = 0, s2 = 0, s3 = 0, playerRow = -1, headers = playerData[0]; for (var i = 1; i < playerData.length; i++) { if (playerData[i][0].toString().replace("'", "") === discordId.toString()) { playerRow = i; s1 = playerData[i][2]||0; s2 = playerData[i][3]||0; s3 = playerData[i][4]||0; break; } } var customVars = []; if (ss.getSheets().length >= 4) { var varData = ss.getSheets()[3].getDataRange().getValues(); for (var v = 1; v < varData.length; v++) { var display = varData[v][0], internal = varData[v][1]; var varMode = varData[v][2] ? varData[v][2].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : ''; // 🌟 C欄:留空=一律顯示/HIDE_ZERO=數值0時不在主列顯示/HIDDEN=一律不在主列顯示(只有背包看得到) if (display && internal) { var val = 0, colIndex = headers.indexOf(internal.toString()); if (colIndex !== -1 && playerRow !== -1) val = playerData[playerRow][colIndex] || 0; customVars.push({ display: display, value: val, mode: varMode }); } } } // 🌟 取得玩家目前持有的身分組名稱(供前端顯示用) // 只顯示在「身分組對照表」裡有填寫名稱的身分組,沒填的(未知身分組)直接不顯示 // 如果呼叫端(例如 getDashboardData)已經算好 userRoles/roleMap 就直接重複使用,不用再重新讀一次表 var userRoleIds = userRoles || getUserRoles(discordId, ss, playerData); var roleMapForDisplay = roleMap || getGuildRoleMap(ss); var roleNames = userRoleIds.map(function(id) { return roleMapForDisplay[id]; }).filter(function(name) { return name; }); return { "status": "success", "found": playerRow !== -1, "s1": s1, "s2": s2, "s3": s3, "customVars": customVars, "roleNames": roleNames }; } // 🌟 把 getScores + getShop 合併成一次請求:只開啟一次試算表、只算一次身分組,前端只需要打一次 API // 比起原本前端同時打兩個各自獨立的請求(getScores、getShop各自重新開啟試算表、各自重新查身分組),這樣能省掉重複的開銷,加快載入速度 function getDashboardData(discordId) { var t0 = new Date().getTime(); var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SHEET_ID); var t1 = new Date().getTime(); var playerData = ss.getSheets()[0].getDataRange().getValues(); // 🌟 只讀一次,給下面userRoles跟scores共用 var t1b = new Date().getTime(); var userRoles = getUserRoles(discordId, ss, playerData); var t2 = new Date().getTime(); var roleMap = getGuildRoleMap(ss); var t3 = new Date().getTime(); var scores = getUserScores(discordId, ss, userRoles, roleMap, playerData); var t4 = new Date().getTime(); var shop = getShopItems(discordId, ss, userRoles, roleMap); var t5 = new Date().getTime(); var timing = { openSpreadsheet_ms: t1 - t0, readPlayerSheet_ms: t1b - t1, getUserRoles_ms: t2 - t1b, getGuildRoleMap_ms: t3 - t2, getUserScores_ms: t4 - t3, getShopItems_ms: t5 - t4, total_ms: t5 - t0 }; return { "status": "success", "scores": scores, "shop": shop, "debugTiming": timing }; } // 🌟 新增週限制計算 (加入 YYYY-ww 的比對) function getPurchaseHistory(historyData, discordId, targetItemName, targetItemId) { var now = new Date(); var todayStr = Utilities.formatDate(now, "GMT+8", "yyyyMMdd"); var weekStr = Utilities.formatDate(now, "GMT+8", "YYYY-ww"); // 例如：2026-27 (第27週) var monthStr = Utilities.formatDate(now, "GMT+8", "yyyyMM"); var stats = { globalDaily: 0, globalWeekly: 0, globalMonthly: 0, personalDaily: 0, personalWeekly: 0, personalMonthly: 0, personalTotal: 0 }; for(var r = 1; r < historyData.length; r++) { var rowItemName = historyData[r][2], rowItemId = historyData[r][4]; var isMatch = false; // 🌟🔧 只要有 itemId 就單純用 ID 比對(商品改名字、ID不變的話,以前的紀錄還是算數,不會因為改名字就把限購重置掉)。 // 只有「連 itemId 都沒存到」的很舊的歷史紀錄(在還沒有商品ID系統之前留下來的),才退回用名稱比對。 if (rowItemId !== undefined && rowItemId !== "") isMatch = (rowItemId.toString() === targetItemId.toString()); else isMatch = (rowItemName === targetItemName); if(isMatch) { var tDate = new Date(historyData[r][0]); var tId = historyData[r][1].toString().replace("'", ""); var tQty = parseInt(historyData[r][3]) || 0; var tDay = Utilities.formatDate(tDate, "GMT+8", "yyyyMMdd"); var tWeek = Utilities.formatDate(tDate, "GMT+8", "YYYY-ww"); var tMonth = Utilities.formatDate(tDate, "GMT+8", "yyyyMM"); if(tId === discordId.toString()) stats.personalTotal += tQty; if(tMonth === monthStr) { stats.globalMonthly += tQty; if(tId === discordId.toString()) stats.personalMonthly += tQty; } if(tWeek === weekStr) { stats.globalWeekly += tQty; if(tId === discordId.toString()) stats.personalWeekly += tQty; } if(tDay === todayStr) { stats.globalDaily += tQty; if(tId === discordId.toString()) stats.personalDaily += tQty; } } } return stats; } // 🌟 一次掃過整張「兌換紀錄」表,把每個商品的限購統計都先算好放進索引(key用 itemId||itemName,沒有itemId的用itemName) // 給 getShopItems 用:原本是「每個商品都重新掃一次全部歷史紀錄」,改成「歷史紀錄只掃一次,每個商品用O(1)查表」 // processPurchase 因為只需要查單一商品,維持用上面的 getPurchaseHistory 即可,沒有索引的必要 function buildHistoryIndex(historyData, discordId) { var now = new Date(); var todayStr = Utilities.formatDate(now, "GMT+8", "yyyyMMdd"); var weekStr = Utilities.formatDate(now, "GMT+8", "YYYY-ww"); var monthStr = Utilities.formatDate(now, "GMT+8", "yyyyMM"); var idStr = discordId.toString(); // 🌟 Utilities.formatDate 是相對昂貴的呼叫,歷史紀錄筆數一多,每一列都呼叫3次會變成新瓶頸 // 用「GMT+8 當天 0 點的整數時間戳」當作快取 key(純數學運算,沒有時區誤判風險,因為GMT+8沒有日光節約時間) // 同一天的紀錄只需要算一次 day/week/month 字串,其餘直接複用結果 var dayPartsCache = {}; function getDateParts(date) { var dayBucket = Math.floor((date.getTime() + 8 * 3600 * 1000) / 86400000); var cached = dayPartsCache[dayBucket]; if (cached) return cached; cached = { day: Utilities.formatDate(date, "GMT+8", "yyyyMMdd"), week: Utilities.formatDate(date, "GMT+8", "YYYY-ww"), month: Utilities.formatDate(date, "GMT+8", "yyyyMM") }; dayPartsCache[dayBucket] = cached; return cached; } var index = {}; for (var r = 1; r < historyData.length; r++) { var rowItemName = historyData[r][2], rowItemId = historyData[r][4]; if (!historyData[r][1]) continue; // 🌟🔧 索引key只用 itemId(有的話),不要再把名稱也綁進去,理由跟 getPurchaseHistory 那邊一樣: // 商品改名字、ID沒變,舊的購買紀錄還是要算進限購統計裡,不能因為改了名字就查不到 var key = (rowItemId !== undefined && rowItemId !== "") ? rowItemId.toString() : rowItemName; if (!index[key]) index[key] = { globalDaily: 0, globalWeekly: 0, globalMonthly: 0, personalDaily: 0, personalWeekly: 0, personalMonthly: 0, personalTotal: 0 }; var entry = index[key]; var tDate = new Date(historyData[r][0]); var tId = historyData[r][1].toString().replace("'", ""); var tQty = parseInt(historyData[r][3]) || 0; var isSelf = (tId === idStr); var parts = getDateParts(tDate); if (isSelf) entry.personalTotal += tQty; if (parts.month === monthStr) { entry.globalMonthly += tQty; if (isSelf) entry.personalMonthly += tQty; } if (parts.week === weekStr) { entry.globalWeekly += tQty; if (isSelf) entry.personalWeekly += tQty; } if (parts.day === todayStr) { entry.globalDaily += tQty; if (isSelf) entry.personalDaily += tQty; } } return index; } function lookupHistoryStats(historyIndex, itemName, itemId) { var key = (itemId !== undefined && itemId !== "" && itemId !== null) ? itemId.toString() : itemName; return historyIndex[key] || { globalDaily: 0, globalWeekly: 0, globalMonthly: 0, personalDaily: 0, personalWeekly: 0, personalMonthly: 0, personalTotal: 0 }; } function getShopItems(discordId, ss, userRoles, roleMap) { ss = ss || SpreadsheetApp.openById(SHEET_ID); var sheet = ss.getSheets()[1], historySheet = ss.getSheets()[2]; var data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues(), historyData = historySheet ? historySheet.getDataRange().getValues() : []; var items = [], now = new Date().getTime(); userRoles = userRoles || getUserRoles(discordId, ss); // 🌟 身分組：取得使用者目前持有的身分組ID roleMap = roleMap || getGuildRoleMap(ss); // 🌟 身分組：取得身分組ID->名稱對照表 var historyIndex = buildHistoryIndex(historyData, discordId); // 🌟 歷史紀錄只整張掃一次,每個商品用O(1)查表,不用各自重新掃整張表 // 🌟 抽獎模式:整張票數紀錄表只掃一次,彙整出「每個商品的加權總票數」跟「我在每個商品裡投了幾張」 var raffleTotalsByItem = {}, raffleMineByItem = {}; var raffleTicketSheetForRead = ss.getSheetByName(RAFFLE_TICKET_SHEET_NAME); if (raffleTicketSheetForRead) { var raffleTicketDataForRead = raffleTicketSheetForRead.getDataRange().getValues(); for (var rtr = 1; rtr < raffleTicketDataForRead.length; rtr++) { var rtrRow = raffleTicketDataForRead[rtr]; if (!rtrRow[0]) continue; var rtrItemId = rtrRow[0].toString(); var rtrUid = rtrRow[1] ? rtrRow[1].toString().replace("'", "") : ''; var rtrWeighted = parseFloat(rtrRow[3]) || 0; var rtrRaw = parseInt(rtrRow[2]) || 0; raffleTotalsByItem[rtrItemId] = (raffleTotalsByItem[rtrItemId] || 0) + rtrWeighted; if (discordId && rtrUid === discordId.toString()) raffleMineByItem[rtrItemId] = { raw: rtrRaw, weighted: rtrWeighted }; } } // 🌟 賭博模式:整張下注紀錄表只掃一次,彙整出「每個商品每個選項的總下注金額」跟「我在每個商品每個選項下注了多少」 var gamblingPoolByItem = {}; // { itemId: { optionName: totalAmount } } var gamblingMineByItem = {}; // { itemId: { optionName: myAmount } } var gamblingBetSheetForRead = ss.getSheetByName(GAMBLING_BET_SHEET_NAME); if (gamblingBetSheetForRead) { var gamblingBetDataForRead = gamblingBetSheetForRead.getDataRange().getValues(); for (var gbr = 1; gbr < gamblingBetDataForRead.length; gbr++) { var gbrRow = gamblingBetDataForRead[gbr]; if (!gbrRow[0]) continue; var gbrItemId = gbrRow[0].toString(); var gbrUid = gbrRow[1] ? gbrRow[1].toString().replace("'", "") : ''; var gbrOption = gbrRow[2] ? gbrRow[2].toString() : ''; var gbrAmount = parseFloat(gbrRow[3]) || 0; if (!gamblingPoolByItem[gbrItemId]) gamblingPoolByItem[gbrItemId] = {}; gamblingPoolByItem[gbrItemId][gbrOption] = (gamblingPoolByItem[gbrItemId][gbrOption] || 0) + gbrAmount; if (discordId && gbrUid === discordId.toString()) { if (!gamblingMineByItem[gbrItemId]) gamblingMineByItem[gbrItemId] = {}; gamblingMineByItem[gbrItemId][gbrOption] = (gamblingMineByItem[gbrItemId][gbrOption] || 0) + gbrAmount; } } } // 🌟 替代貨幣(例如拍賣幣)折抵功能：需要查玩家目前持有的各貨幣餘額,這裡先掃一次玩家表 var playerSheetForAlt = ss.getSheets()[0]; var playerDataForAlt = playerSheetForAlt.getDataRange().getValues(); var playerHeadersForAlt = playerDataForAlt[0]; var playerRowForAlt = -1; for (var pa = 1; pa < playerDataForAlt.length; pa++) { if (playerDataForAlt[pa][0] && playerDataForAlt[pa][0].toString().replace("'", "") === discordId.toString()) { playerRowForAlt = pa; break; } } function getAltBalance_(altCurrencyName) { if (!altCurrencyName || playerRowForAlt === -1) return 0; var colIdx = playerHeadersForAlt.indexOf(altCurrencyName); if (colIdx === -1) return 0; return parseInt(playerDataForAlt[playerRowForAlt][colIdx]) || 0; } // 🌟 密碼鎖定功能:先掃一次解鎖記錄,整理出這位玩家「已經永久解鎖過」的分類/商品清單 var unlockedCategories = {}, unlockedItemIds = {}; var unlockLogSheet = ss.getSheetByName(UNLOCK_LOG_SHEET_NAME); if (unlockLogData[ul][2] === 'CATEGORY') unlockedCategories[ulTarget] = true; else if (unlockLogData[ul][2] === 'ITEM') unlockedItemIds[ulTarget] = true; } } } var categoryLockSheet = ss.getSheetByName(CATEGORY_LOCK_SHEET_NAME); var categoryLockData = categoryLockSheet ? categoryLockSheet.getDataRange().getValues() : []; function getCategoryLocked_(categoryName) { for (var cl = 1; cl < categoryLockData.length; cl++) { if (categoryLockData[cl][0] && categoryLockData[cl][0].toString().trim() === categoryName) { var hasFixed = categoryLockData[cl][1] && categoryLockData[cl][1].toString().trim() !== ''; var hasCode = categoryLockData[cl][2] && categoryLockData[cl][2].toString().trim() !== ''; var hasMode = categoryLockData[cl][7] && categoryLockData[cl][7].toString().trim() !== ''; var hasRotating = hasMode && ( (categoryLockData[cl][8] && categoryLockData[cl][8].toString().trim() !== '') || (categoryLockData[cl][9] && categoryLockData[cl][9].toString().trim() !== '') ); return (hasFixed || hasCode || hasRotating); } } return false; } function getCategoryLockVisibility_(categoryName) { for (var cl = 1; cl < categoryLockData.length; cl++) { if (categoryLockData[cl][0] && categoryLockData[cl][0].toString().trim() === categoryName) { return categoryLockData[cl][4] ? categoryLockData[cl][4].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : ''; } } return ''; } // 🌟 分類鎖的持續性(留空=永久解鎖/SESSION=每次都要重新輸入),判斷「之前解鎖過」的紀錄現在還算不算數要用到 function getCategoryLockPersistent_(categoryName) { for (var cl = 1; cl < categoryLockData.length; cl++) { if (categoryLockData[cl][0] && categoryLockData[cl][0].toString().trim() === categoryName) { return categoryLockData[cl][3] ? categoryLockData[cl][3].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : ''; } } return ''; } function getCategoryLockShowHint_(categoryName) { for (var cl = 1; cl < categoryLockData.length; cl++) { if (categoryLockData[cl][0] && categoryLockData[cl][0].toString().trim() === categoryName) { return categoryLockData[cl][5] ? categoryLockData[cl][5].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : ''; } } return ''; } function getCategoryLockHintText_(categoryName) { for (var cl = 1; cl < categoryLockData.length; cl++) { if (categoryLockData[cl][0] && categoryLockData[cl][0].toString().trim() === categoryName) { return categoryLockData[cl][6] ? categoryLockData[cl][6].toString() : ''; } } return ''; } var categoryOrder = []; if (ss.getSheets().length >= 6) { var catSheet = ss.getSheets()[5]; var catData = catSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); for (var c = 1; c < catData.length; c++) { if (catData[c][0]) categoryOrder.push(catData[c][0].toString().trim()); } } // 🌟 「選一群組」功能：同一組裡只要選了其中一個商品,其他的就會被鎖住; // 解鎖時機不是另外設定週期,而是直接看「之前選的那個商品」自己的個人限購(I/J/L/M欄)有沒有重置、現在能不能再買一次 // 第一步:先掃一次商品表,記下每個有設定群組的商品屬於哪個群組、以及它自己的個人限購設定 var groupItemInfo = {}; // key: itemId(沒有itemId才退回用name) -> {group, itemName, itemId, limitPD, limitPW, limitPM, limitPT} for (var g = 1; g < data.length; g++) { var gName = data[g][0]; if (!gName) continue; var groupNameRaw = data[g][20] ? data[g][20].toString().trim() : ''; if (groupNameRaw) { var gItemId = data[g][18] ? data[g][18].toString().trim() : ''; // 🌟🔧 key只用ID(有的話),不要再把名稱綁進去:商品改名字、ID沒變,還是要算同一個商品,不然改名後互斥群組就鎖不住了 var gKey = gItemId || gName; groupItemInfo[gKey] = { group: groupNameRaw, itemName: gName, itemId: gItemId, limitPD: data[g][8] !== "" && data[g][8] !== undefined ? parseInt(data[g][8]) : Infinity, limitPW: data[g][11] !== "" && data[g][11] !== undefined ? parseInt(data[g][11]) : Infinity, limitPM: data[g][9] !== "" && data[g][9] !== undefined ? parseInt(data[g][9]) : Infinity, limitPT: data[g][12] !== "" && data[g][12] !== undefined ? parseInt(data[g][12]) : Infinity, }; } } // 第二步:掃一次歷史紀錄,記下這個玩家在每個群組裡,曾經選過哪些商品(用Set,因為可能換過不只一個) var myGroupHistoryKeys = {}; // 群組名稱 -> { 商品key: true, ... } for (var h = 1; h < historyData.length; h++) { var hRow = historyData[h]; if (!hRow[1]) continue; var info = groupItemInfo[hKey]; if (info) { if (!myGroupHistoryKeys[info.group]) myGroupHistoryKeys[info.group] = {}; myGroupHistoryKeys[info.group][hKey] = true; } } for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) { var name = data[i][0] ? data[i][0].toString() : ''; // 🌟🔧 強制轉字串:商品名稱如果剛好是純數字(例如「88」),Google Sheets會自動存成數字型態,後面的.indexOf()是字串專用方法,不轉型會直接炸掉整個列表 if (!name) continue; if (name.indexOf("[測試]") !== -1 && ADMIN_IDS.indexOf(discordId.toString()) === -1) { continue; } var itemStatus = data[i][22] ? data[i][22].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : ''; // W(22) 狀態:DRAFT=草稿,不對玩家顯示 if (itemStatus === 'DRAFT') continue; var itemId = data[i][18] ? data[i][18].toString().trim() : ""; // S(18) if (!itemId) { itemId = Utilities.getUuid().split('-')[0].toUpperCase(); sheet.getRange(i + 1, 19).setValue(itemId); } var price = parseInt(data[i][1]) || 0; var startDate = dateColTime_(data[i][2]), endDate = dateColTime_(data[i][3]); var limitPD = data[i][8] !== "" && data[i][8] !== undefined ? parseInt(data[i][8]) : Infinity; var limitPM = data[i][9] !== "" && data[i][9] !== undefined ? parseInt(data[i][9]) : Infinity; var limitGW = data[i][10] !== "" && data[i][10] !== undefined ? parseInt(data[i][10]) : Infinity; // K(10) 全服一周 var limitPW = data[i][11] !== "" && data[i][11] !== undefined ? parseInt(data[i][11]) : Infinity; // L(11) 個人一周 var limitPT = data[i][12] !== "" && data[i][12] !== undefined ? parseInt(data[i][12]) : Infinity; // M(12) 終身 var rawCurrency = data[i][13] ? data[i][13].toString().trim() : '升階2'; // N(13) var displayCurrency = (rawCurrency === '升階2') ? '幻彩水晶' : rawCurrency; var rewardVar = data[i][14] ? data[i][14].toString().trim() : ""; // O(14) var rawRewardQty = data[i][15] ? data[i][15].toString().trim() : ""; // P(15) var imageUrl = data[i][16] ?
