data[i][28].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : ''; var itemLockHintText = data[i][29] ? data[i][29].toString() : ''; var lockPasswordMode = data[i][30] ? data[i][30].toString().trim() : ''; var lockPasswordSeed = data[i][31] ? data[i][31].toString().trim() : ''; var lockPasswordSchedule = data[i][32] ? data[i][32].toString().trim() : ''; var itemLocked = !!(lockFixedPassword || lockCodeName || (lockPasswordMode && (lockPasswordSeed || lockPasswordSchedule))); // 🌟 賭博模式:AQ(42)=是否為賭博商品, AR(43)=賠率模式(FIXED固定賠率/POOL集資池), AS(44)=下注選項與賠率, // AT(45)=輸家退還比例(0-100,留空=0=全輸不退), AU(46)=開獎結果JSON(系統寫入,有值代表已經宣布結果), // AV(47)=集資池賠率鎖定方式(留空/FINAL=依最終結算總額計算,BETTIME=以下注當下的即時賠率為主,鎖定不受之後池子變化影響) var isGambling = data[i][42] ? data[i][42].toString().trim().toUpperCase() === 'TRUE' : false; var gamblingOddsMode = data[i][43] ? data[i][43].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : 'FIXED'; if (gamblingOddsMode !== 'POOL') gamblingOddsMode = 'FIXED'; var gamblingOptionsRaw = data[i][44] ? data[i][44].toString().trim() : ''; var gamblingLoserRefundPercent = data[i][45] !== '' && data[i][45] !== undefined ? parseFloat(data[i][45]) : 0; var gamblingResultRaw = data[i][46] ? data[i][46].toString().trim() : ''; var gamblingResult = gamblingResultRaw ? safeParseJSON_(gamblingResultRaw) : null; var gamblingPoolLockMode = data[i][47] ? data[i][47].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : 'FINAL'; if (gamblingPoolLockMode !== 'BETTIME') gamblingPoolLockMode = 'FINAL'; // 🌟 AX(49)=最高賠率上限(只對「下注當下鎖定」模式有效,留空=不封頂;算出來的賠率超過這個值就自動封頂,避免池子太薄時出現誇張倍率) var gamblingMaxOdds = data[i][49] !== '' && data[i][49] !== undefined ? parseFloat(data[i][49]) : 0; if (!(gamblingMaxOdds > 0)) gamblingMaxOdds = 0; // 0 代表不封頂 var gamblingOptions = [], gamblingMyBets = null, gamblingTotalPool = 0; if (isGambling) { var gamblingOptionsList = parseGamblingOptions_(gamblingOptionsRaw); var gPoolForItem = gamblingPoolByItem[itemId] || {}; var gMineForItem = gamblingMineByItem[itemId] || {}; gamblingOptionsList.forEach(function (opt) { var poolAmt = gPoolForItem[opt.name] || 0; gamblingTotalPool += poolAmt; }); gamblingOptions = gamblingOptionsList.map(function (opt) { var poolAmt = gPoolForItem[opt.name] || 0; // 🌟 集資池模式的「目前隱含賠率」= 全場總下注 ÷ 這個選項的總下注(給玩家下注前參考) // BETTIME模式:這個公式要跟實際下注時鎖定用的公式完全一致(都是「下注前」的池子狀態,不含這筆金額本身), // 這個選項還沒人下注過就用選項數量當參考值,不管其他選項有沒有人下注,這樣顯示的參考值才會等於等一下真正鎖定的賠率。 // FINAL模式:純粹資訊性顯示,這個選項沒人下注就維持顯示「尚無人下注」即可。 var impliedOdds; if (gamblingOddsMode === 'POOL' && gamblingPoolLockMode === 'BETTIME') { impliedOdds = poolAmt > 0 ? Math.round((gamblingTotalPool / poolAmt) * 100) / 100 : gamblingOptionsList.length; if (gamblingMaxOdds > 0 && impliedOdds > gamblingMaxOdds) impliedOdds = gamblingMaxOdds; // 🌟 封頂 } else if (gamblingOddsMode === 'POOL') { if (gamblingTotalPool > 0 && poolAmt > 0) impliedOdds = Math.round((gamblingTotalPool / poolAmt) * 100) / 100; else if (gamblingTotalPool === 0) impliedOdds = gamblingOptionsList.length; // 🌟 都還沒人下注:參考值=選項數量(假設均分) else impliedOdds = null; // 其他選項有人下注、但這個選項還沒人下注:維持顯示「尚無人下注」 } else { impliedOdds = null; } // 🌟 下注比率:這個選項佔全場總下注金額的百分比,兩種賠率模式都適用,單純給玩家看「大家都押哪邊」 var poolPercent = gamblingTotalPool > 0 ? Math.round((poolAmt / gamblingTotalPool) * 10000) / 100 : 0; return { name: opt.name, odds: opt.odds, // 固定賠率模式才有意義 pool: poolAmt, // 這個選項目前總共下注了多少(兩種模式都顯示,集資池模式用來算機率/賠率參考) poolPercent: poolPercent, // 🌟 這個選項佔全場總下注的比率(%) impliedOdds: impliedOdds, // 🌟 集資池模式目前的即時賠率(僅供參考;BETTIME模式下注當下才會真正鎖定) myBet: gMineForItem[opt.name] || 0, isWinner: gamblingResult ? (gamblingResult.winningOption === opt.name) : null, }; }); gamblingMyBets = gMineForItem; } // 🌟 抽獎模式:AN(39)=是否為抽獎商品, AO(40)=身分組加權清單, AP(41)=開獎結果JSON(系統寫入) var isRaffle = data[i][39] ? data[i][39].toString().trim().toUpperCase() === 'TRUE' : false; var raffleRoleWeights = data[i][40] ? data[i][40].toString().trim() : ''; var raffleResultRaw = data[i][41] ? data[i][41].toString().trim() : ''; var raffleWinners = raffleResultRaw ? safeParseJSON_(raffleResultRaw) : null; var raffleMultiplier = 1, raffleMyRaw = 0, raffleMyWeighted = 0, raffleTotalWeighted = 0, raffleOdds = 0; if (isRaffle) { raffleMultiplier = getRaffleMultiplier_(userRoles, parseRaffleWeights_(raffleRoleWeights)); var raffleMine = raffleMineByItem[itemId] || { raw: 0, weighted: 0 }; raffleMyRaw = raffleMine.raw; raffleMyWeighted = raffleMine.weighted; raffleTotalWeighted = raffleTotalsByItem[itemId] || 0; raffleOdds = raffleTotalWeighted > 0 ? Math.round((raffleMyWeighted / raffleTotalWeighted) * 10000) / 100 : 0; } // 🌟 SESSION 模式(每次都要重新輸入)要忽略「之前(可能是還在永久解鎖模式時)留下的舊解鎖紀錄」,不能因為過去解鎖過就一直算數 var itemUnlocked = !itemLocked || (itemPersistentRaw !== 'SESSION' && !!unlockedItemIds[itemId]); var categoryLocked = getCategoryLocked_(category); var categoryPersistentRaw = getCategoryLockPersistent_(category); var categoryUnlocked = !categoryLocked || (categoryPersistentRaw !== 'SESSION' && !!unlockedCategories[category]); var categoryLockVisibility = getCategoryLockVisibility_(category); var categoryLockShowHint = getCategoryLockShowHint_(category); var categoryLockHintText = getCategoryLockHintText_(category); var isUnlimitedStock = (stockValue === "" || stockValue === "無限" || stockValue === "無限制"); var baseStock = isUnlimitedStock ? Infinity : parseInt(stockValue); var historyStats = lookupHistoryStats(historyIndex, name, itemId); var remainGD = limitGD - historyStats.globalDaily, remainGM = limitGM - historyStats.globalMonthly, remainGW = limitGW - historyStats.globalWeekly; var remainPD = limitPD - historyStats.personalDaily, remainPM = limitPM - historyStats.personalMonthly, remainPW = limitPW - historyStats.personalWeekly; var remainPT = limitPT - historyStats.personalTotal; var effectiveStock = Math.min(baseStock, remainGD, remainGW, remainGM, remainPD, remainPW, remainPM, remainPT); // 🌟 累積兌換次數里程碑獎勵:AM(38)=規則(多行文字,格式「次數 => 獎勵」),算給玩家看目前進度用。 // 「每N」重複里程碑沒有「已達成就不會再出現」這回事,永遠會有下一個倍數;一次性的里程碑達成後就不再顯示。 // 所有規則裡,挑「下一次會觸發的門檻」最接近目前累積數的那一個顯示給玩家看。 var milestones = parseMilestoneRules(data[i][38]); var nextMilestone = null; for (var mi2 = 0; mi2 < milestones.length; mi2++) { var m = milestones[mi2]; if (m.isGacha) { // 🌟 盲盒式里程碑:獎池裡如果全部項目都設了庫存且都發完了,才視為沒得抽了、不顯示 var poolAllOut = m.gachaPool.length > 0 && m.gachaPool.every(function(p) { return p.stock !== null && p.stock <= 0; }); if (poolAllOut) continue; } else if (m.stock !== null && m.stock <= 0) continue; // 🌟 庫存已經發完的里程碑不再顯示,不然玩家會一直期待一個永遠拿不到的獎勵 var nextCount; if (m.repeat) nextCount = (Math.floor(historyStats.personalTotal / m.count) + 1) * m.count; else { if (historyStats.personalTotal >= m.count) continue; nextCount = m.count; } var previewText = m.isGacha ? '神秘獎勵(隨機抽獎)' : m.rewardText; if (nextMilestone === null || nextCount < nextMilestone.count) nextMilestone = { count: nextCount, rewardText: previewText, repeat: m.repeat, isGacha: !!m.isGacha, gachaPool: m.isGacha ? m.gachaPool : null }; } // 🌟 給玩家看的完整里程碑清單(不只是下一個,全部都列出來,含目前狀態) var milestoneList = milestones.map(function(m) { var poolExhausted = m.isGacha ? (m.gachaPool.length > 0 && m.gachaPool.every(function(p) { return p.stock !== null && p.stock <= 0; })) : (m.stock !== null && m.stock <= 0); return { count: m.count, repeat: !!m.repeat, isGacha: !!m.isGacha, rewardText: m.isGacha ? '神秘獎勵(隨機抽獎)' : m.rewardText, gachaPool: m.isGacha ? m.gachaPool : null, stock: m.isGacha ? null : m.stock, achieved: m.repeat ? null : (historyStats.personalTotal >= m.count), // 🌟 一次性才有「已達成」的概念,重複性的用 timesTriggered 表示 timesTriggered: m.repeat ? Math.floor(historyStats.personalTotal / m.count) : (historyStats.personalTotal >= m.count ? 1 : 0), exhausted: poolExhausted, }; }); var gachaPool = []; if (rewardVar === "" && rawRewardQty !== "" && rawRewardQty !== "0") { gachaPool = parseGachaRules(rawRewardQty); if (!isRaffle) { var hasInfinite = false, totalGachaStock = 0; for (var p = 0; p < gachaPool.length; p++) { if (gachaPool[p].stock === null) hasInfinite = true; else totalGachaStock += gachaPool[p].stock; } if (!hasInfinite) effectiveStock = Math.min(effectiveStock, totalGachaStock); } } var state = "available", stateMsg = "可兌換"; if (startDate && now < startDate) { state = "not_started"; stateMsg = "尚未開始"; } else if (endDate && now > endDate) { state = "ended"; stateMsg = "活動結束"; } else if (effectiveStock <= 0) { state = "sold_out"; stateMsg = "達到上限/已抽完"; } // 🌟 抽獎模式:已經開獎過就直接鎖住(不能再投票),還沒開獎但時間到了就顯示等待開獎 if (isRaffle) { if (raffleWinners) { state = "raffle_drawn"; stateMsg = "🏆 已開獎"; } else if (state === "ended") { stateMsg = "⌛ 已截止，等待開獎"; } } // 🌟 賭博模式:管理員已經宣布結果就直接鎖住(不能再下注),截止但還沒宣布結果就顯示等待中 if (isGambling) { if (gamblingResult) { state = "gambling_settled"; stateMsg = "🎲 已公布結果"; } else if (state === "ended") { stateMsg = "⌛ 已截止下注，等待管理員公布結果"; } } // 🌟 身分組限定檢查：只有在其他狀態都正常(可兌換)時才檢查身分組,優先顯示售完/未開始等訊息 var requiredRoleNames = []; var roleRequirementMode = 'ANY'; var roleRequirementMinCount = 1; if (requiredRoleStr) { var roleReq = parseRoleRequirement(requiredRoleStr); roleRequirementMode = roleReq.mode; roleRequirementMinCount = roleReq.minCount; for (var rI = 0; rI < roleReq.ids.length; rI++) requiredRoleNames.push(roleMap[roleReq.ids[rI]] || ('未知身分組' + roleReq.ids[rI])); } var hasRolePermission = checkRolePermission(userRoles, requiredRoleStr); if (state === "available" && !hasRolePermission) { state = "no_permission"; stateMsg = "身分組不符"; } // 🌟 選一群組檢查：玩家已經選過同群組的其他商品、且那個商品自己的個人限購還沒重置時鎖住 // (優先順序在身分組之後,只有原本狀態正常才覆蓋) var exclusiveGroup = data[i][20] ? data[i][20].toString().trim() : ''; // U(20) 選一群組 var myItemKey = itemId ? (itemId + '||' + name) : name; var groupLocked = false; if (exclusiveGroup && myGroupHistoryKeys[exclusiveGroup]) { var chosenKeys = Object.keys(myGroupHistoryKeys[exclusiveGroup]); for (var ck = 0; ck < chosenKeys.length; ck++) { var chosenKey = chosenKeys[ck]; if (chosenKey === myItemKey) continue; // 自己買過自己不算被群組鎖,交給自己的限購欄位處理就好 var chosenInfo = groupItemInfo[chosenKey]; if (!chosenInfo) continue; // 商品可能後來被刪除/改名,找不到限購規則就不鎖,避免永久卡死 var chosenStats = lookupHistoryStats(historyIndex, chosenInfo.itemName, chosenInfo.itemId); var stillBlocked = false; if (chosenInfo.limitPD === Infinity && chosenInfo.limitPW === Infinity && chosenInfo.limitPM === Infinity && chosenInfo.limitPT === Infinity) { stillBlocked = true; // 那個商品完全沒設個人限購 = 沒有重置依據,維持永久鎖 } else { if (chosenInfo.limitPD !== Infinity && (chosenInfo.limitPD - chosenStats.personalDaily) <= 0) stillBlocked = true; if (chosenInfo.limitPW !== Infinity && (chosenInfo.limitPW - chosenStats.personalWeekly) <= 0) stillBlocked = true; if (chosenInfo.limitPM !== Infinity && (chosenInfo.limitPM - chosenStats.personalMonthly) <= 0) stillBlocked = true; if (chosenInfo.limitPT !== Infinity && (chosenInfo.limitPT - chosenStats.personalTotal) <= 0) stillBlocked = true; } if (stillBlocked) { groupLocked = true; break; } } } if (state === "available" && groupLocked) { state = "group_locked"; stateMsg = "已選擇同組其他商品"; } var limitsInfo = { baseStock: isUnlimitedStock ? "無限" : baseStock, remainGD: limitGD === Infinity ? null : remainGD, remainGW: limitGW === Infinity ? null : remainGW, remainGM: limitGM === Infinity ? null : remainGM, remainPD: limitPD === Infinity ? null : remainPD, remainPW: limitPW === Infinity ? null : remainPW, remainPM: limitPM === Infinity ? null : remainPM, remainPT: limitPT === Infinity ? null : remainPT, effectiveStock: effectiveStock === Infinity ? "無限" : effectiveStock }; items.push({ id: itemId, name: name, price: price, state: state, stateMsg: stateMsg, category: category, limits: limitsInfo, currency: rawCurrency, displayCurrency: displayCurrency, imageUrl: imageUrl, remark: remark, gachaPool: gachaPool, startDate: startDate, endDate: endDate, requiredRoleNames: requiredRoleNames, hasRolePermission: hasRolePermission, // 🌟 身分組限定資訊 roleRequirementMode: roleRequirementMode, roleRequirementMinCount: roleRequirementMinCount, exclusiveGroup: exclusiveGroup, groupLocked: groupLocked, // 🌟 選一群組資訊 sortOrder: data[i][21] !== '' && data[i][21] !== undefined ? parseInt(data[i][21]) : null, // V(21) 顯示順序,越小越前面 altCurrency: altCurrency, altCurrencyRate: altCurrencyRate, altCurrencyBalance: altCurrencyBalance, // 🌟 替代貨幣折抵資訊(向下相容,只有第一種) altCurrencies: altCurrencies, // 🌟 完整的多種替代貨幣清單 [{name,rate,balance}, ...] extraCost: extraCost, // 🌟 額外必付費用清單 [{name,amount}, ...](每次購買都一定要一起收,不是選填折抵) milestones: milestoneList, nextMilestone: nextMilestone, personalTotalPurchased: historyStats.personalTotal, // 🌟 累積兌換次數里程碑獎勵資訊 itemLocked: itemLocked, itemUnlocked: itemUnlocked, categoryLocked: categoryLocked, categoryUnlocked: categoryUnlocked, // 🌟 密碼鎖定資訊 itemLockVisibility: itemLockVisibility, categoryLockVisibility: categoryLockVisibility, // 🌟 解鎖前顯示模式 categoryLockShowHint: categoryLockShowHint, // 🌟 分類完全隱藏時,側邊欄要不要顯示這個分類 itemLockHintText: itemLockHintText, categoryLockHintText: categoryLockHintText, // 🌟 密碼提示詞 isRaffle: isRaffle, raffleMultiplier: raffleMultiplier, // 🌟 抽獎模式資訊 raffleMyRawTickets: raffleMyRaw, raffleMyWeightedTickets: raffleMyWeighted, raffleTotalWeightedTickets: raffleTotalWeighted, raffleOdds: raffleOdds, raffleWinners: raffleWinners, isGambling: isGambling, gamblingOddsMode: gamblingOddsMode, gamblingOptions: gamblingOptions, // 🌟 賭博模式資訊 gamblingLoserRefundPercent: gamblingLoserRefundPercent, gamblingTotalPool: gamblingTotalPool, gamblingResult: gamblingResult, gamblingMaxOdds: gamblingMaxOdds, gamblingPoolLockMode: gamblingPoolLockMode, }); } // 🌟 依顯示順序排序(數字越小越前面;沒設定的商品維持原本在試算表裡的相對順序,排在有設定順序的商品後面) items.sort(function(a, b) { var oa = a.sortOrder === null ? Infinity : a.sortOrder; var ob = b.sortOrder === null ? Infinity : b.sortOrder; return oa - ob; }); return { "status": "success", "items": items, "categoryOrder": categoryOrder }; } function processPurchase(discordId, itemId, qty, altMode, altAmountParam, unlockPassword, altSelected, gamblingOption, expectedGamblingOdds) { var lock = LockService.getScriptLock(); lock.waitLock(10000); try { var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SHEET_ID); var playerSheet = ss.getSheets()[0], shopSheet = ss.getSheets()[1], historySheet = ss.getSheets()[2]; var shopData = shopSheet.getDataRange().getValues(), historyData = historySheet.getDataRange().getValues(); var keySheet = ss.getSheets().length >= 5 ? ss.getSheets()[4] : null; var keyData = keySheet ? keySheet.getDataRange().getValues() : []; var shopRowIndex = -1; for (var i = 1; i < shopData.length; i++) { if (shopData[i][18] && shopData[i][18].toString().trim() === itemId.toString()) { // ID shopRowIndex = i; break; } } if (shopRowIndex === -1) return { "status": "error", "message": "找不到該商品！(可能已下架或 ID 變更)" }; var itemName = shopData[shopRowIndex][0], pricePerItem = parseInt(shopData[shopRowIndex][1]) || 0; var itemStatusForBuy = shopData[shopRowIndex][22] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][22].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : ''; if (itemStatusForBuy === 'DRAFT') return { "status": "error", "message": "此商品尚未上架(草稿狀態)，無法兌換" }; // 🌟 密碼鎖定檢查:分類鎖先檢查,再檢查商品自己的鎖(兩者都要通過才能購買) var itemCategoryForLock = shopData[shopRowIndex][5] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][5].toString().trim() : ''; var categoryLockCfg = getCategoryLockConfig_(ss, itemCategoryForLock); var categoryLockResult = checkUnlock_(ss, discordId, 'CATEGORY', itemCategoryForLock, categoryLockCfg.fixedPassword, categoryLockCfg.codeName, categoryLockCfg.persistent, unlockPassword, categoryLockCfg.passwordMode, categoryLockCfg.passwordSeed, categoryLockCfg.passwordSchedule, categoryLockCfg.guessLimitEnabled, categoryLockCfg.guessLimitCount, categoryLockCfg.guessLimitPeriod); if (categoryLockResult.locked && !categoryLockResult.unlocked) { return { "status": "error", "message": categoryLockResult.message, "needUnlock": "CATEGORY" }; } var itemFixedPassword = shopData[shopRowIndex][25] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][25].toString() : ''; // Z(25) var itemCodeName = shopData[shopRowIndex][26] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][26].toString() : ''; // AA(26) var itemPersistent = shopData[shopRowIndex][27] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][27].toString() : ''; // AB(27) var itemPasswordMode = shopData[shopRowIndex][30] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][30].toString() : ''; // AE(30) 🌟 自動輪替密碼週期 var itemPasswordSeed = shopData[shopRowIndex][31] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][31].toString() : ''; // AF(31) 🌟 自動輪替密碼種子 var itemPasswordSchedule = shopData[shopRowIndex][32] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][32].toString() : ''; // AG(32) 🌟 自訂密碼表 var itemGuessLimitEnabled = shopData[shopRowIndex][33] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][33].toString() : ''; // AH(33) 🌟 是否開啟每日猜測次數上限 var itemGuessLimitCount = shopData[shopRowIndex][34] ? parseInt(shopData[shopRowIndex][34], 10) || 0 : 0; // AI(34) 🌟 每期最多可猜幾次 var itemGuessLimitPeriod = shopData[shopRowIndex][35] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][35].toString() : 'DAILY'; // AJ(35) 🌟 次數上限重置週期 var itemLockResult = checkUnlock_(ss, discordId, 'ITEM', itemId, itemFixedPassword, itemCodeName, itemPersistent, unlockPassword, itemPasswordMode, itemPasswordSeed, itemPasswordSchedule, itemGuessLimitEnabled, itemGuessLimitCount, itemGuessLimitPeriod); if (itemLockResult.locked && !itemLockResult.unlocked) { return { "status": "error", "message": itemLockResult.message, "needUnlock": "ITEM" }; } if (itemName.indexOf("[測試]") !== -1 && ADMIN_IDS.indexOf(discordId.toString()) === -1) { return { "status": "error", "message": "此為測試專用物品，您無權限兌換！" }; } // 🌟 身分組限定檢查：後端再驗證一次,避免前端被繞過 var requiredRoleStr = shopData[shopRowIndex][19] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][19].toString().trim() : ''; if (requiredRoleStr) { var userRolesForCheck = getUserRoles(discordId, ss); if (!checkRolePermission(userRolesForCheck, requiredRoleStr)) { var roleMapForCheck = getGuildRoleMap(ss); var roleReqForCheck = parseRoleRequirement(requiredRoleStr); var reqNames = roleReqForCheck.ids.map(function(id) { return roleMapForCheck[id] || id; }); var reqHint = ""; if (roleReqForCheck.mode === 'ALL') reqHint = "需全部持有："; else if (roleReqForCheck.mode === 'COUNT') reqHint = "需持有其中至少 " + roleReqForCheck.minCount + " 個："; else reqHint = "需持有其中任一個："; return { "status": "error", "message": "您沒有兌換此商品所需的身分組(" + reqHint + reqNames.join("、") + ")" }; } } // 🌟 選一群組檢查：後端再驗證一次,避免前端被繞過(直接打API硬買群組裡的第二個商品) var exclusiveGroup = shopData[shopRowIndex][20] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][20].toString().trim() : ''; if (exclusiveGroup) { var myItemKeyForCheck = itemId ? itemId.toString() : itemName; // 先建立「商品key -> 群組+自己的個人限購設定」對照表(只收有設定群組的商品) var groupItemInfoForCheck = {}; for (var gc = 1; gc < shopData.length; gc++) { var gcName = shopData[gc][0]; if (!gcName) continue; var gcGroup = shopData[gc][20] ? shopData[gc][20].toString().trim() : ''; if (gcGroup) { var gcItemId = shopData[gc][18] ? shopData[gc][18].toString().trim() : ''; // 🌟🔧 key只用ID(有的話),不要再把名稱綁進去,理由跟上面 getShopItems 那邊一樣 var gcKey = gcItemId || gcName; groupItemInfoForCheck[gcKey] = { group: gcGroup, itemName: gcName, itemId: gcItemId, limitPD: shopData[gc][8] !== "" && shopData[gc][8] !== undefined ? parseInt(shopData[gc][8]) : Infinity, limitPW: shopData[gc][11] !== "" && shopData[gc][11] !== undefined ? parseInt(shopData[gc][11]) : Infinity, limitPM: shopData[gc][9] !== "" && shopData[gc][9] !== undefined ? parseInt(shopData[gc][9]) : Infinity, limitPT: shopData[gc][12] !== "" && shopData[gc][12] !== undefined ? parseInt(shopData[gc][12]) : Infinity, }; } } // 再掃歷史紀錄,找出這個玩家在這個群組裡曾經選過哪些「別的」商品 var chosenKeysForCheck = {}; for (var hc = 1; hc < historyData.length; hc++) { var hcRow = historyData[hc]; if (!hcRow[1]) continue; if (hcRow[1].toString().replace("'", "") !== discordId.toString()) continue; var hcItemName = hcRow[2], hcItemId = hcRow[4]; var hcKey = (hcItemId !== undefined && hcItemId !== "") ? hcItemId.toString() : hcItemName; if (groupItemInfoForCheck[hcKey] && groupItemInfoForCheck[hcKey].group === exclusiveGroup && hcKey !== myItemKeyForCheck) { chosenKeysForCheck[hcKey] = true; } } // 針對每個曾經選過的商品,檢查它自己的個人限購是否還沒重置(還沒重置才繼續鎖住) for (var chosenKeyCheck in chosenKeysForCheck) { var chosenInfoCheck = groupItemInfoForCheck[chosenKeyCheck]; var chosenStatsCheck = getPurchaseHistory(historyData, discordId, chosenInfoCheck.itemName, chosenInfoCheck.itemId); var stillBlockedCheck = false; if (chosenInfoCheck.limitPD === Infinity && chosenInfoCheck.limitPW === Infinity && chosenInfoCheck.limitPM === Infinity && chosenInfoCheck.limitPT === Infinity) { stillBlockedCheck = true; } else { if (chosenInfoCheck.limitPD !== Infinity && (chosenInfoCheck.limitPD - chosenStatsCheck.personalDaily) <= 0) stillBlockedCheck = true; if (chosenInfoCheck.limitPW !== Infinity && (chosenInfoCheck.limitPW - chosenStatsCheck.personalWeekly) <= 0) stillBlockedCheck = true; if (chosenInfoCheck.limitPM !== Infinity && (chosenInfoCheck.limitPM - chosenStatsCheck.personalMonthly) <= 0) stillBlockedCheck = true; if (chosenInfoCheck.limitPT !== Infinity && (chosenInfoCheck.limitPT - chosenStatsCheck.personalTotal) <= 0) stillBlockedCheck = true; } if (stillBlockedCheck) { return { "status": "error", "message": "您已經在「" + exclusiveGroup + "」這個選一群組裡選擇過其他商品（" + chosenInfoCheck.itemName + "），該商品的限購尚未重置，無法再兌換此商品。" }; } } } var startDate = dateColTime_(shopData[shopRowIndex][2]), endDate = dateColTime_(shopData[shopRowIndex][3]); var stockValue = shopData[shopRowIndex][4]; var now = new Date().getTime(); if (startDate && now < startDate) return { "status": "error", "message": "活動尚未開始！" }; if (endDate && now > endDate) return { "status": "error", "message": "活動已經結束！" }; var limitGD = shopData[shopRowIndex][6] !== "" && shopData[shopRowIndex][6] !== undefined ? parseInt(shopData[shopRowIndex][6]) : Infinity; var limitGM = shopData[shopRowIndex][7] !== "" && shopData[shopRowIndex][7] !== undefined ? parseInt(shopData[shopRowIndex][7]) : Infinity; var limitPD = shopData[shopRowIndex][8] !== "" && shopData[shopRowIndex][8] !== undefined ? parseInt(shopData[shopRowIndex][8]) : Infinity; var limitPM = shopData[shopRowIndex][9] !== "" && shopData[shopRowIndex][9] !== undefined ? parseInt(shopData[shopRowIndex][9]) : Infinity; var limitGW = shopData[shopRowIndex][10] !== "" && shopData[shopRowIndex][10] !== undefined ? parseInt(shopData[shopRowIndex][10]) : Infinity; var limitPW = shopData[shopRowIndex][11] !== "" && shopData[shopRowIndex][11] !== undefined ? parseInt(shopData[shopRowIndex][11]) : Infinity; var limitPT = shopData[shopRowIndex][12] !== "" && shopData[shopRowIndex][12] !== undefined ? parseInt(shopData[shopRowIndex][12]) : Infinity; var currencyName = shopData[shopRowIndex][13] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][13].toString().trim() : '升階2'; // 🌟 抽獎模式:AN(39)=是否為抽獎商品, AO(40)=身分組加權清單, AP(41)=開獎結果JSON(系統寫入,有值代表已開獎) var isRaffle = shopData[shopRowIndex][39] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][39].toString().trim().toUpperCase() === 'TRUE' : false; var raffleRoleWeights = shopData[shopRowIndex][40] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][40].toString().trim() : ''; var raffleResultRaw = shopData[shopRowIndex][41] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][41].toString().trim() : ''; if (isRaffle && raffleResultRaw) return { "status": "error", "message": "此抽獎活動已經開獎，無法再投票" }; // 🌟 賭博模式:AQ(42)=是否為賭博商品, AR(43)=賠率模式, AS(44)=下注選項與賠率, AT(45)=輸家退還比例, AU(46)=開獎結果JSON, AV(47)=集資池賠率鎖定方式 var isGambling = shopData[shopRowIndex][42] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][42].toString().trim().toUpperCase() === 'TRUE' : false; var gamblingOddsModeForBuy = shopData[shopRowIndex][43] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][43].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : 'FIXED'; if (gamblingOddsModeForBuy !== 'POOL') gamblingOddsModeForBuy = 'FIXED'; var gamblingOptionsRaw = shopData[shopRowIndex][44] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][44].toString().trim() : ''; var gamblingResultRawForBuy = shopData[shopRowIndex][46] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][46].toString().trim() : ''; var gamblingPoolLockModeForBuy = shopData[shopRowIndex][47] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][47].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : 'FINAL'; if (gamblingPoolLockModeForBuy !== 'BETTIME') gamblingPoolLockModeForBuy = 'FINAL'; // 🌟 AX(49)=最高賠率上限(只對「下注當下鎖定」模式有效,留空/0=不封頂) var gamblingMaxOddsForBuy = shopData[shopRowIndex][49] !== '' && shopData[shopRowIndex][49] !== undefined ? parseFloat(shopData[shopRowIndex][49]) : 0; if (!(gamblingMaxOddsForBuy > 0)) gamblingMaxOddsForBuy = 0; var gamblingOptionsParsedForBuy = isGambling ? parseGamblingOptions_(gamblingOptionsRaw) : []; if (isGambling) { if (gamblingResultRawForBuy) return { "status": "error", "message": "這場賭博已經公布結果了，無法再下注" }; var gOptTrim = (gamblingOption || '').toString().trim(); if (!gOptTrim) return { "status": "error", "message": "請選擇要下注的選項" }; var gOptValid = gamblingOptionsParsedForBuy.some(function (o) { return o.name === gOptTrim; }); if (!gOptValid) return { "status": "error", "message": "找不到這個下注選項，請重新整理頁面再試一次" }; } // 🌟 替代貨幣折抵(可多種同時開放,例如拍賣幣、活動幣):X(23)=替代貨幣欄位名稱(可逗號分隔多個), Y(24)=匯率(逗號分隔,跟X欄一一對應) var altCurrencies = parseAltCurrencies_(shopData[shopRowIndex][23], shopData[shopRowIndex][24]); var altSelectedNames = (altSelected || '').toString().split(',').map(function(s) { return s.trim(); }).filter(Boolean); var rewardVar = shopData[shopRowIndex][14] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][14].toString().trim() : ""; var rawRewardQty = shopData[shopRowIndex][15] ? shopData[shopRowIndex][15].toString().trim() : ""; var isUnlimited = (stockValue === "" || stockValue === "無限" || stockValue === "無限制"); var baseStock = isUnlimited ? Infinity : parseInt(stockValue); var historyStats = getPurchaseHistory(historyData, discordId, itemName, itemId); var remainGD = limitGD - historyStats.globalDaily, remainGM = limitGM - historyStats.globalMonthly, remainGW = limitGW - historyStats.globalWeekly; var remainPD = limitPD - historyStats.personalDaily, remainPM = limitPM - historyStats.personalMonthly, remainPW = limitPW - historyStats.personalWeekly; var remainPT = limitPT - historyStats.personalTotal; var effectiveStock = Math.min(baseStock, remainGD, remainGW, remainGM, remainPD, remainPW, remainPM, remainPT); if (!isRaffle && !isGambling && rewardVar === "" && rawRewardQty !== "" && rawRewardQty !== "0") { var gachaPoolForCheck = parseGachaRules(rawRewardQty); var hasInfinite = false, totalGachaStock = 0; for (var p = 0; p < gachaPoolForCheck.length; p++) { if (gachaPoolForCheck[p].stock === null) hasInfinite = true; else totalGachaStock += gachaPoolForCheck[p].stock; } if (!hasInfinite) effectiveStock = Math.min(effectiveStock, totalGachaStock); } if (effectiveStock < qty) return { "status": "error", "message": "超過限購數量或盲盒已被抽完！" }; var isKeyItem = itemName.indexOf("[序號]") !== -1, isHoldCheck = itemName.indexOf("[持有]") !== -1; var availableKeyRows = []; if (isKeyItem) { if (keySheet) { var uniqueKeyNames = []; for (var k = 1; k < keyData.length; k++) { var kn = keyData[k][0] ? keyData[k][0].toString().trim() : ""; if (kn && uniqueKeyNames.indexOf(kn) === -1) uniqueKeyNames.push(kn); } var cleanNameForMatch = itemName.replace(/\[.*?\]/g, '').trim(); var targetKeyName = ""; for (var u = 0; u < uniqueKeyNames.length; u++) { if (cleanNameForMatch.indexOf(uniqueKeyNames[u]) !== -1) { if (uniqueKeyNames[u].length > targetKeyName.length) { targetKeyName = uniqueKeyNames[u]; } } } if (targetKeyName === "") { return { "status": "error", "message": "系統錯誤：找不到符合此商品名稱的序號類別！請確認序號庫的 A 欄是否有對應名稱。" }; } for (var k = 1; k < keyData.length; k++) { var rowKeyName = keyData[k][0] ? '幻彩水晶' : currencyName; var extraCostList = parseExtraCost_(shopData[shopRowIndex][36], shopData[shopRowIndex][37]); // 🌟 AK(36)=額外費用幣種(逗號分隔), AL(37)=額外費用數量(逗號分隔,跟AK一一對應) var actualDeduct = 0; // 🌟 替代貨幣折抵(可多種同時折抵):usedAltList = 這次實際折抵到的幣種明細 [{name, rate, amount, colIndex}, ...] var usedAltList = []; var extraCostApplied = []; // 🌟 這次購買實際要收的額外費用明細 [{name, amount, colIndex}, ...] if (isHoldCheck) { if (totalCost < 0) { if (currentBalance >= totalCost) return { "status": "error", "message": "未達領取條件！" + displayCurrencyName + " 必須低於 " + totalCost + " 才能領取" }; } else { if (currentBalance < totalCost) return { "status": "error", "message": "未達領取條件！需要持有至少 " + totalCost + " " + displayCurrencyName }; } actualDeduct = 0; } else { var remainingCost = totalCost; if (altCurrencies.length > 0 && altMode && altMode !== 'none' && totalCost > 0 && altSelectedNames.length > 0) { var multiUsage = computeMultiAltUsage_(totalCost, altCurrencies, altMode, altSelectedNames, altAmountParam, function(curName) { var idx = playerHeaders.indexOf(curName); if (idx === -1) return 0; return parseInt(playerData[playerRow - 1][idx]) || 0; }); if (multiUsage.error) return { "status": "error", "message": multiUsage.error }; remainingCost = multiUsage.mainNeeded; for (var au = 0; au < multiUsage.used.length; au++) { var altColIdx = playerHeaders.indexOf(multiUsage.used[au].name); if (altColIdx === -1) return { "status": "error", "message": "系統錯誤：找不到替代貨幣欄位 [" + multiUsage.used[au].name + "]" }; usedAltList.push({ name: multiUsage.used[au].name, rate: multiUsage.used[au].rate, amount: multiUsage.used[au].amount, colIndex: altColIdx }); } } // 🌟 額外必付費用(例如「水晶2+水晶碎片30」):不是玩家可以選要不要用的折抵,是每次購買都一定要一起收的貨幣 for (var ec = 0; ec < extraCostList.length; ec++) { var ecItem = extraCostList[ec]; var ecColIdx = playerHeaders.indexOf(ecItem.name); if (ecColIdx === -1) return { "status": "error", "message": "系統錯誤：找不到額外費用的貨幣欄位 [" + ecItem.name + "]" }; var ecNeeded = ecItem.amount * qty; var ecBalance = parseInt(playerData[playerRow - 1][ecColIdx]) || 0; if (ecBalance < ecNeeded) return { "status": "error", "message": ecItem.name + " 不足！這個商品還需要 " + ecNeeded + " " + ecItem.name }; extraCostApplied.push({ name: ecItem.name, amount: ecNeeded, colIndex: ecColIdx }); } var altSummaryForError = usedAltList.length > 0 ? usedAltList.map(function(u) { return u.amount + ' ' + u.name; }).join('、') : ''; if (currentBalance < remainingCost) return { "status": "error", "message": displayCurrencyName + " 餘額不足！" + (altSummaryForError ? "(已折抵 " + altSummaryForError + ")" : "") }; actualDeduct = remainingCost; } // 🌟 賭博模式(集資池+下注當下賠率鎖定):在真正扣款前,先重新算一次「如果現在下注會鎖定的賠率」, // 跟玩家畫面上顯示、送出下注時附帶回來的 expectedGamblingOdds 比對,不一樣就直接拒絕(此時還沒扣過錢,不用退款)。 // 這樣可以避免玩家看到的賠率跟實際成交的賠率「貨不對版」(例如送出的當下,剛好被別人插隊下注改變了池子)。 if (isGambling && gamblingOddsModeForBuy === 'POOL' && gamblingPoolLockModeForBuy === 'BETTIME' && expectedGamblingOdds !== '' && expectedGamblingOdds !== undefined) { var gPreCheckSheet = ss.getSheetByName(GAMBLING_BET_SHEET_NAME); var gPreCheckData = gPreCheckSheet ? gPreCheckSheet.getDataRange().getValues() : []; var gPreTotalPool = 0, gPreOptionPool = 0; for (var gpc = 1; gpc < gPreCheckData.length; gpc++) { if (gPreCheckData[gpc][0] && gPreCheckData[gpc][0].toString() === itemId.toString()) { var gpcAmt = parseFloat(gPreCheckData[gpc][3]) || 0; gPreTotalPool += gpcAmt; if (gPreCheckData[gpc][2] && gPreCheckData[gpc][2].toString() === gOptTrim) gPreOptionPool += gpcAmt; } } var gCurrentOdds; if (gPreOptionPool === 0) { // 🌟 跟下面實際下注時的邏輯一致:這個選項還沒人下注過,參考/鎖定賠率用選項數量,不要算出無限大或0 gCurrentOdds = gamblingOptionsParsedForBuy.length; } else { gCurrentOdds = Math.round((gPreTotalPool / gPreOptionPool) * 100) / 100; } if (gamblingMaxOddsForBuy > 0 && gCurrentOdds > gamblingMaxOddsForBuy) gCurrentOdds = gamblingMaxOddsForBuy; // 🌟 封頂 var gExpectedOddsNum = Math.round(parseFloat(expectedGamblingOdds) * 100) / 100; if (isNaN(gExpectedOddsNum) || Math.abs(gCurrentOdds - gExpectedOddsNum) > 0.01) { return { "status": "error", "message": "賠率已經變動(目前約 x" + gCurrentOdds.toFixed(2) + " 倍,跟您看到的 x" + parseFloat(expectedGamblingOdds).toFixed(2) + " 倍不同),可能是剛好有別人也下注了。請重新整理頁面確認最新賠率後再下注。", "oddsChanged": true, "newOdds": gCurrentOdds }; } } // 🌟 統一用「欄位 -> 要扣多少」的表一次結算,不管主要貨幣/折抵替代幣/額外費用有沒有剛好用到同一個欄位都一定會正確加總,不會互相蓋掉 var deductMap = {}; function addDeduct_(colIdx, amt) { deductMap[colIdx] = (deductMap[colIdx] || 0) + amt; } addDeduct_(currencyColIndex, actualDeduct); usedAltList.forEach(function(u) { addDeduct_(u.colIndex, u.amount); }); extraCostApplied.forEach(function(e) { addDeduct_(e.colIndex, e.amount); }); for (var deductColKey in deductMap) { var deductColIdx = parseInt(deductColKey, 10); var deductCurBal = parseInt(playerData[playerRow - 1][deductColIdx]) || 0; var deductNewBal = deductCurBal - deductMap[deductColKey]; playerSheet.getRange(playerRow, deductColIdx + 1).setValue(deductNewBal); playerData[playerRow - 1][deductColIdx] = deductNewBal; } if (!isUnlimited) shopSheet.getRange(shopRowIndex + 1, 5).setValue(baseStock - qty); // 🌟 抽獎模式:買=投票,不進入下面的扣庫存/發獎流程,獎勵留到開獎時才統一發放 if (isRaffle) { var raffleTicketSheet = ss.getSheetByName(RAFFLE_TICKET_SHEET_NAME); if (!raffleTicketSheet) { raffleTicketSheet = ss.insertSheet(RAFFLE_TICKET_SHEET_NAME); raffleTicketSheet.appendRow(['商品ID', 'DiscordID', '原始票數', '加權票數', '最後更新時間']); } var raffleTicketData = raffleTicketSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); var raffleTicketRowIdx = -1; for (var rt = 1; rt < raffleTicketData.length; rt++) { if (raffleTicketData[rt][0] && raffleTicketData[rt][0].toString() === itemId.toString() && raffleTicketData[rt][1] && raffleTicketData[rt][1].toString().replace("'", "") === discordId.toString()) { raffleTicketRowIdx = rt + 1; break; } } var raffleUserRoles = getUserRoles(discordId, ss, playerData); var raffleMultiplier = getRaffleMultiplier_(raffleUserRoles, parseRaffleWeights_(raffleRoleWeights)); var raffleWeightedGain = qty * raffleMultiplier; if (raffleTicketRowIdx === -1) { raffleTicketSheet.appendRow([itemId, "'" + discordId.toString(), qty, raffleWeightedGain, new Date()]); } else { var raffleExistingRaw = parseInt(raffleTicketData[raffleTicketRowIdx - 1][2]) || 0; var raffleExistingWeighted = parseFloat(raffleTicketData[raffleTicketRowIdx - 1][3]) || 0; raffleTicketSheet.getRange(raffleTicketRowIdx, 3, 1, 3).setValues([[raffleExistingRaw + qty, raffleExistingWeighted + raffleWeightedGain, new Date()]]); } var raffleBalanceAfter = playerData[playerRow - 1][currencyColIndex]; var raffleAltCostSummary = usedAltList.map(function (u) { return u.name + " -" + u.amount; }).join("、"); var raffleExtraCostSummary = extraCostApplied.map(function (e) { return e.name + " -" + e.amount; }).join("、"); historySheet.appendRow([ new Date(), discordId.toString(), itemName, qty, itemId, "", "🎟️投入" + qty + "張(加權" + raffleWeightedGain + "張)", currentBalance, raffleBalanceAfter, raffleAltCostSummary, raffleExtraCostSummary, "" // 🌟 J替代貨幣扣款 | K額外費用扣款 | L總共獲得(抽獎投票沒有立即發獎,留空) ]); // 🌟🔧 同樣改成跟一般購買相容的 "[購買] discordId 商品名|額外資訊 數量 花費 貨幣" 格式,理由跟賭博下注那邊一致 var raffleMsg = "[購買] " + discordId + " " + itemName + "|投入" + qty + "張(加權x" + raffleMultiplier + "=" + raffleWeightedGain + "張) " + qty + " " + actualDeduct + " " + displayCurrencyName; usedAltList.forEach(function (u) { raffleMsg += " " + u.name + " " + (-u.amount); }); extraCostApplied.forEach(function (e) { raffleMsg += " " + e.name + " " + (-e.amount); }); queueWebhook_(raffleMsg); return { "status": "success", "message": "已投入 " + qty + " 張抽獎券！(加權倍率 x" + raffleMultiplier + "，實際計為 " + raffleWeightedGain + " 張)", "isRaffle": true, "cost": actualDeduct, "costCurrencyName": displayCurrencyName }; } // 🌟 賭博模式:買=下注,不進入下面的扣庫存/發獎流程,結果留到管理員手動公布時才統一結算發放 if (isGambling) { var gamblingBetSheet = ss.getSheetByName(GAMBLING_BET_SHEET_NAME); if (!gamblingBetSheet) { gamblingBetSheet = ss.insertSheet(GAMBLING_BET_SHEET_NAME); gamblingBetSheet.appendRow(['商品ID', 'DiscordID', '選項', '下注金額', '賠率金額乘積累計(集資池鎖定模式用)', '最後更新時間']); } var gBetData = gamblingBetSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); var gBetRowIdx = -1; var gOptFinal = (gamblingOption || '').toString().trim(); for (var gb = 1; gb < gBetData.length; gb++) { if (gBetData[gb][0] && gBetData[gb][0].toString() === itemId.toString() && gBetData[gb][1] && gBetData[gb][1].toString().replace("'", "") === discordId.toString() && gBetData[gb][2] && gBetData[gb][2].toString() === gOptFinal) { gBetRowIdx = gb + 1; break; } } // 🌟🔧🔥 重要修正:下注的「賭注金額」要用商品的**原價總額**(qty×price=totalCost),不能用實際扣的主要貨幣(actualDeduct)! // 玩家如果用替代貨幣(例如幻彩水晶碎片)折抵掉部分或全部費用,actualDeduct 會變得很小甚至是0, // 但玩家「投入的價值」其實還是 totalCost 那麼多——賭注份量、賠率計算、最後結算能拿多少,都應該以這個真實投入的價值為準, // 不然玩家花了替代貨幣折抵,下注卻完全不算數(等於白花了折抵的錢,賠率算出x1.1卻永遠只能拿到0)。 var gBetCost = totalCost; // 🌟 這才是這筆下注真正的賭注金額(不管實際上是用主要貨幣、替代貨幣、還是兩者混合支付的) // 🌟🔧 集資池「以下注當下賠率為主」模式:賠率是看「下注前」的池子狀態算出來的(不含這筆金額本身), // 這樣同一筆下注不管金額多少,倍率都一樣(下注100跟下注1000鎖定的倍率相同,差別只在拿到的錢等比例變多)。 // 不能把這筆金額也算進分母/分子,不然數量一改倍率就跟著變,而且金額越大倍率越差,不合理。 var gOddsAmountProductGain = 0; if (gamblingOddsModeForBuy === 'POOL' && gamblingPoolLockModeForBuy === 'BETTIME') { var gTotalPoolBefore = 0, gOptionPoolBefore = 0; for (var gp = 1; gp < gBetData.length; gp++) { if (gBetData[gp][0] && gBetData[gp][0].toString() === itemId.toString()) { var gpAmt = parseFloat(gBetData[gp][3]) || 0; gTotalPoolBefore += gpAmt; if (gBetData[gp][2] && gBetData[gp][2].toString() === gOptFinal) gOptionPoolBefore += gpAmt; } } var gOddsAtBetTime; if (gOptionPoolBefore === 0) { // 🌟 這個選項目前還沒人下注過(不管其他選項有沒有人下注):用「假設均分」當鎖定賠率(=選項數量), // 不要算出無限大或0,第一個押這個選項的人統一給這個保底參考值 gOddsAtBetTime = gamblingOptionsParsedForBuy.length; } else { gOddsAtBetTime = gTotalPoolBefore / gOptionPoolBefore; } if (gamblingMaxOddsForBuy > 0 && gOddsAtBetTime > gamblingMaxOddsForBuy) gOddsAtBetTime = gamblingMaxOddsForBuy; // 🌟 封頂,避免池子太薄時鎖定到誇張倍率 gOddsAmountProductGain = gBetCost * gOddsAtBetTime; } if (gBetRowIdx === -1) { gamblingBetSheet.appendRow([itemId, "'" + discordId.toString(), gOptFinal, gBetCost, gOddsAmountProductGain, new Date()]); } else { var gExistingAmount = parseFloat(gBetData[gBetRowIdx - 1][3]) || 0; var gExistingProduct = parseFloat(gBetData[gBetRowIdx - 1][4]) || 0; gamblingBetSheet.getRange(gBetRowIdx, 4, 1, 3).setValues([[gExistingAmount + gBetCost, gExistingProduct + gOddsAmountProductGain, new Date()]]); } var gBalanceAfter = playerData[playerRow - 1][currencyColIndex]; var gAltCostSummary = usedAltList.map(function (u) { return u.name + " -" + u.amount; }).join("、"); var gExtraCostSummary = extraCostApplied.map(function (e) { return e.name + " -" + e.amount; }).join("、"); // 🌟 算出這筆下注的賠率/潛在獲利資訊,寫進歷史紀錄裡,玩家自己看得到「投了多少倍率、贏了大概能拿多少」 var gPotentialInfo = ''; if (gamblingOddsModeForBuy === 'FIXED') { var gFixedOptCfg = null; for (var gfo = 0; gfo < gamblingOptionsParsedForBuy.length; gPotentialInfo = "（賠率x" + gFixedOdds + "，若中獎可得 " + gFixedPotential + " " + displayCurrencyName + "）"; } else if (gamblingPoolLockModeForBuy === 'BETTIME') { var gLockedOddsRounded = Math.round(gOddsAtBetTime * 100) / 100; var gLockedPotential = Math.floor(gOddsAmountProductGain); gPotentialInfo = "（已鎖定賠率x" + gLockedOddsRounded + "，若中獎可得 " + gLockedPotential + " " + displayCurrencyName + "）"; } else { gPotentialInfo = "（集資池模式，實際賠率依最終結算，若中獎至少拿回本金）"; } historySheet.appendRow([ new Date(), discordId.toString(), itemName, qty, itemId, "", "🎲下注「" + gOptFinal + "」" + gBetCost + " " + displayCurrencyName + gPotentialInfo, currentBalance, gBalanceAfter, gAltCostSummary, gExtraCostSummary, "" ]); // 🌟🔧 這裡的格式一定要跟一般購買的 "[購買] discordId 商品名|額外資訊 數量 花費 貨幣" 完全一致, // Skript(瓜.sk)才能正確解析出 <@discordId> 提及、暱稱、跟正確的花費/貨幣顯示,不然會顯示成原始數字ID、 // 或欄位對不上位置變成 (之前用自訂格式「[賭博下注] ...」就是這樣壞掉的)。 // 🔥 注意:這裡的「花費」欄位要用 actualDeduct(實際從主要貨幣扣了多少),不能用 gBetCost(下注的名目賭注金額)—— // 如果玩家用替代貨幣折抵掉部分/全部費用,gBetCost 跟 actualDeduct 會不一樣,Skript 那邊要同步的是「主要貨幣真正被扣多少」, // 折抵掉的部分已經另外用 usedAltList 那段附加上去了。 var gMsg = "[購買] " + discordId + " " + itemName + "|下注「" + gOptFinal + "」 " + qty + " " + actualDeduct + " " + displayCurrencyName; usedAltList.forEach(function (u) { gMsg += " " + u.name + " " + (-u.amount); }); extraCostApplied.forEach(function (e) { gMsg += " " + e.name + " " + (-e.amount); }); queueWebhook_(gMsg); return { "status": "success", "message": "已下注「" + gOptFinal + "」，投入賭注 " + gBetCost + " " + displayCurrencyName + "！結果將在管理員公布後統一結算。", "isGambling": true, "cost": actualDeduct, "costCurrencyName": displayCurrencyName, "stakeValue": gBetCost }; } var assignedKeys = []; if (isKeyItem && keySheet) { for (var q = 0; q < qty; q++) { var rowToUse = availableKeyRows[q]; var keyVal = keySheet.getRange(rowToUse, 2).getValue(); assignedKeys.push(keyVal); } } if (totalStock > 0) { var kRoll = Math.random() * totalStock, kCum = 0; for(var i=0; i 0) wonItem = fallbacks[Math.floor(Math.random() * fallbacks.length)]; } if (wonItem) { drawnItemsList.push(wonItem.dispName); }).join("、"); var totalRewardsSummary = (resultStrs || []).join("、"); historySheet.appendRow([ new Date(), discordId.toString(), itemName, qty, itemId, keysString, drawnResultStr, currentBalance, balanceAfter, altCostSummary, // 🌟 J 替代貨幣扣款明細,例如「拍賣幣 -10」,同時折抵多種就用「、」分隔 extraCostSummary, // 🌟 K 額外必付費用扣款明細,格式同上 totalRewardsSummary // 🌟 L 這次總共獲得的所有變數(盲盒抽多次時同一種變數已加總),格式「變數名 數量」用「、」分隔 ]); if (displayExt !== "") { finalItemName = cleanItemName + "|" + displayExt; } // 🌟 累積兌換次數里程碑獎勵:這次購買完成後,個人累積購買數量從 oldTotal 變成 newTotal, // 中間跨過的每一個里程碑都要發獎(一次買很多件、一口氣跨過好幾個里程碑的話,會全部一起發)。 // 「每N」的重複里程碑如果一次跨過好幾個倍數(例如每5,一次買到從第3件變第18件,中間跨過5/10/15三個倍數),也會一次全部發完。 // 如果某個里程碑的獎勵發不出來(例如序號庫存不足),不會讓整筆已經完成的購買失敗,只會記錄下來讓管理員知道要補發、並停止繼續發同一條規則(避免同樣的錯誤一直重複記錄)。 // 🌟 有標庫存的里程碑,發完就沒有了(即使玩家累積數量已經到門檻,庫存用完後也不會再發),庫存扣減結果會寫回試算表。 // 🌟 盲盒式里程碑(獎池格式):達成時從獎池抽一個,抽獎邏輯、機率/庫存判斷都跟商品本身的盲盒完全共用同一套函式。 var milestoneRewardsGranted = [], milestoneRewardErrors = []; var milestoneStockChanged = false; // 🌟 發一次里程碑獎勵(不管是盲盒式或固定式),回傳 {error} 或 {rewardText, resultStrs} function grantOneMilestone_(ms) { if (ms.isGacha) { var wonItem = drawOneFromGachaPool_(ms.gachaPool); if (!wonItem) return { error: "獎池目前沒有可中獎的項目(機率沒中、庫存也不足,請聯絡管理員補充)" }; milestoneStockChanged = true; // 🌟 就算沒中庫存類獎項,drawOneFromGachaPool_ 也可能扣到別的項目庫存,保守一律標記需要寫回 var grantResultG = grantVarListToPlayer_(wonItem.varList, playerHeaders, playerData, playerRow, playerSheet, keySheet, keyData, discordId, assignedKeys); if (grantResultG.error) return { error: grantResultG.error }; return { rewardText: wonItem.dispName, resultStrs: grantResultG.resultStrs }; } if (ms.stock !== null && ms.stock <= 0) return { error: "「" + ms.rewardText + "」庫存已發完,請聯絡管理員補貨" }; var grantResult = grantVarListToPlayer_(ms.varList, playerHeaders, playerData, playerRow, playerSheet, keySheet, keyData, discordId, assignedKeys); if (grantResult.error) return { error: grantResult.error }; if (ms.stock !== null) { ms.stock -= 1; milestoneStockChanged = true; } return { rewardText: ms.rewardText, resultStrs: grantResult.resultStrs }; } if (!isHoldCheck) { var milestoneRules = parseMilestoneRules(shopData[shopRowIndex][38]); if (milestoneRules.length > 0) { var msOldTotal = historyStats.personalTotal; var msNewTotal = msOldTotal + qty; for (var mi = 0; mi < milestoneRules.length; mi++) { var ms = milestoneRules[mi]; if (ms.repeat) { var timesCrossed = Math.floor(msNewTotal / ms.count) - Math.floor(msOldTotal / ms.count); for (var tc = 0; tc < timesCrossed; tc++) { var milestoneNumber = (Math.floor(msOldTotal / ms.count) + tc + 1) * ms.count; var grantResultR = grantOneMilestone_(ms); if (grantResultR.error) { milestoneRewardErrors.push("累積第 " + milestoneNumber + " 次里程碑獎勵：" + grantResultR.error); break; } milestoneRewardsGranted.push({ count: milestoneNumber, rewardText: grantResultR.rewardText, repeat: true, resultStrs: grantResultR.resultStrs }); } } else if (ms.count > msOldTotal && ms.count <= msNewTotal) { var grantResult = grantOneMilestone_(ms); if (grantResult.error) milestoneRewardErrors.push("累積第 " + ms.count + " 次里程碑獎勵：" + grantResult.error); else milestoneRewardsGranted.push({ count: ms.count, rewardText: grantResult.rewardText, repeat: false, resultStrs: grantResult.resultStrs }); } } if (milestoneStockChanged) shopSheet.getRange(shopRowIndex + 1, 39).setValue(serializeMilestoneRules(milestoneRules)); // AM(39,1-based) 寫回扣過庫存的規則 } } var msg = "[購買] " + discordId + " " + finalItemName + " " + qty + " " + webhookCost + " " + displayCurrencyName; }), "milestoneErrors": milestoneRewardErrors }; } finally { lock.releaseLock(); flushPendingWebhooks_(); } } // ============================================================ // 🎰 抽獎模式:自動開獎排程 / 管理員手動開獎 / 投票名單查詢 // (商品後台編輯畫面勾選「抽獎模式」即可,不需要另外建立獨立的抽獎活動工作表; // 只有「抽獎票數紀錄」這張表是系統自動建立與寫入的,不用手動建立) // ============================================================ // 🌟 系統排程:每隔幾分鐘檢查一次「商品」工作表,時間到就自動開獎 // (要到 Apps Script「觸發條件」設定時間驅動觸發器指到這個函式) function checkAndDrawShopRaffles() { var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SHEET_ID); var shopSheet = ss.getSheets()[1]; var data = shopSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); var now = new Date().getTime(); for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) { var row = data[i]; if (!row[0]) continue; var isRaffle = row[39] ? row[39].toString().trim().toUpperCase() === 'TRUE' : false; if (!isRaffle) continue; var alreadyDrawn = row[41] ? row[41].toString().trim() : ''; if (alreadyDrawn) continue; // 已經開過獎了 var endDate = row[3] ? new Date(row[3]).getTime() : null; if (!endDate || now < endDate) continue; // 時間還沒到 drawShopRaffle_(ss, i + 1); } } // 🌟 開一個抽獎商品的獎(依加權票數抽出中獎者;獎池格式沿用盲盒規則,支援多獎項/多得獎人; // 發獎邏輯直接重用 grantVarListToPlayer_,跟商品盲盒/里程碑發獎是同一套函式,幻彩水晶雙欄位/序號庫/非即時都會一致處理) function drawShopRaffle_(ss, sheetRowNum) { var lock = LockService.getScriptLock(); lock.waitLock(20000); try { var shopSheet = ss.getSheets()[1]; var latestRow = shopSheet.getRange(sheetRowNum, 1, 1, 42).getValues()[0]; var alreadyDrawn = latestRow[41] ? latestRow[41].toString().trim() : ''; if (alreadyDrawn) return; // 避免觸發器重疊執行造成重複開獎 var itemName = latestRow[0]; var itemId = latestRow[18] ? latestRow[18].toString().trim() : ''; var rawRewardQty = latestRow[15] ? latestRow[15].toString().trim() : ''; var ticketSheet = ss.getSheetByName(RAFFLE_TICKET_SHEET_NAME); var ticketData = ticketSheet ? ticketSheet.getDataRange().getValues() : []; var entries = []; // {discordId, weighted} var totalWeighted = 0; for (var t = 1; t < ticketData.length; t++) { if (!ticketData[t][0] || ticketData[t][0].toString() !== itemId) continue; var uid = ticketData[t][1].toString().replace("'", ""); var w = parseFloat(ticketData[t][3]) || 0; if (w <= 0) continue; entries.push({ discordId: uid, weighted: w }); totalWeighted += w; } var pool = rawRewardQty ? parseGachaRules(rawRewardQty) : []; if (entries.length === 0 || pool.length === 0) { shopSheet.getRange(sheetRowNum, 42).setValue(JSON.stringify({ note: '無人投票或未設定獎池,活動自動關閉' })); queueWebhook_('⚠️ 抽獎商品【' + itemName + '】時間已到,但無人投票或未設定獎池,已自動關閉。'); return; } var playerSheet = ss.getSheets()[0]; var playerData = playerSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); var playerHeaders = playerData[0]; var winners = []; var keySheet = ss.getSheets().length >= 5 ? ss.getSheets()[4] : null; var keyData = keySheet ? keySheet.getDataRange().getValues() : []; // 一個獎項 = 抽出對應份數的中獎人(沒填份數的獎項當作抽1位);同一人可能重複中獎,除非自己控管獎池設計 for (var p = 0; p < pool.length; p++) { var prize = pool[p]; var drawTimes = (prize.stock === null) ? 1 : prize.stock; for (var s = 0; s < drawTimes; s++) { if (entries.length === 0) break; var roll = Math.random() * totalWeighted, cum = 0, winnerIdx = entries.length - 1; for (var e = 0; e < entries.length; e++) { cum += entries[e].weighted; if (roll <= cum) { winnerIdx = e; break; } } var winner = entries[winnerIdx]; var winnerPlayerRow = -1; for (var wp = 1; wp < playerData.length; wp++) { if (playerData[wp][0].toString().replace("'", "") === winner.discordId.toString()) { winnerPlayerRow = wp + 1; break; } } if (winnerPlayerRow === -1) { queueWebhook_('⚠️ 系統錯誤:抽獎中獎者 <@' + winner.discordId + '> 已不在玩家表中'); } else { var varList = (prize.varList && prize.varList.length > 0) ? prize.varList : [{ varName: prize.varName, qty: prize.qty }]; var grantResult = grantVarListToPlayer_(varList, playerHeaders, playerData, winnerPlayerRow, playerSheet, keySheet, keyData, winner.discordId, []); if (grantResult.error) { queueWebhook_('⚠️ <@' + winner.discordId + '> 中獎「' + prize.dispName + '」但發放失敗:' + grantResult.error); } else { // 🌟🔧 這裡直接寫試算表發獎,Skript(瓜.sk)自己那份貨幣變數不會跟著動,一定要另外送一則 // "[購買]" 格式同步訊息,把 resultStrs 裡每一組「變數名 數量」都附加上去,它才會照著加到自己的變數 var raffleCurrencyPairs = (grantResult.resultStrs || []).filter(function (s) { return s.indexOf('[序號]') === -1 && s.indexOf('[非即時]') === -1 && s.indexOf('[身分組]') === -1; }); if (raffleCurrencyPairs.length > 0) { var raffleSyncMsg = "[購買] " + winner.discordId + " " + itemName + "|抽獎中獎「" + prize.dispName + "」 1 0 幻彩水晶 " + raffleCurrencyPairs.join(" "); try { queueWebhook_(raffleSyncMsg); } catch (e) {} } } } winners.push({ discordId: winner.discordId, prize: prize.dispName }); } } shopSheet.getRange(sheetRowNum, 42).setValue(JSON.stringify(winners)); var announce = '🎉 抽獎商品【' + itemName + '】已自動開獎!\n' + winners.map(function (w) { return '🏆 <@' + w.discordId + '> 獲得「' + w.prize + '」'; }).join('\n'); queueWebhook_(announce); } finally { lock.releaseLock(); flushPendingWebhooks_(); } } // 🌟 管理員手動立即開獎某個抽獎商品(不用等時間到,方便測試或臨時提前開獎) function adminDrawShopRaffleNow(discordId, params) { if (!isAdmin_(discordId)) return { status: 'error', message: '權限不足' }; var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SHEET_ID); var shopSheet = ss.getSheets()[1]; var data = shopSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); var rowIdx = -1; for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) { if (data[i][18] && data[i][18].toString().trim() === params.itemId.toString()) { rowIdx = i + 1; break; } } if (rowIdx === -1) return { status: 'error', message: '找不到此商品' }; var isRaffle = data[rowIdx - 1][39] ? data[rowIdx - 1][39].toString().trim().toUpperCase() === 'TRUE' : false; if (!isRaffle) return { status: 'error', message: '這不是抽獎模式的商品' }; drawShopRaffle_(ss, rowIdx); return { status: 'success', message: '已執行開獎!' }; } // 🌟 取得某個抽獎商品的完整投票名單(玩家前台跟後台管理共用同一支,依加權票數由高到低排序) function getRaffleParticipants(itemId) { var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SHEET_ID); var ticketSheet = ss.getSheetByName(RAFFLE_TICKET_SHEET_NAME); if (!ticketSheet) return { status: 'success', totalWeighted: 0, list: [] }; var ticketData = ticketSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); var playerData = ss.getSheets()[0].getDataRange().getValues(); var entries = [], totalWeighted = 0; for (var t = 1; t < ticketData.length; t++) { if (!ticketData[t][0] || ticketData[t][0].toString() !== itemId.toString()) continue; var uid = ticketData[t][1] ? ticketData[t][1].toString().replace("'", "") : ''; if (!uid) continue; var raw = parseInt(ticketData[t][2]) || 0; var weighted = parseFloat(ticketData[t][3]) || 0; if (weighted <= 0) continue; entries.push({ discordId: uid, name: getPlayerDisplayName_(uid, ss, playerData) || uid, raw: raw, weighted: weighted, }); totalWeighted += weighted; } entries.forEach(function (e) { e.odds = totalWeighted > 0 ? Math.round((e.weighted / totalWeighted) * 10000) / 100 : 0; }); entries.sort(function (a, b) { return b.weighted - a.weighted; }); return { status: 'success', totalWeighted: totalWeighted, list: entries }; } // ============================================================ // 🎲 賭博模式:下注名單查詢(給後台結算前參考用) / 管理員手動公布結果並結算發放 // ============================================================ // 🌟 取得某個賭博商品目前每一筆下注明細(依選項分組會由前端自己做,這裡回傳原始清單) function adminGetGamblingBets(discordId, params) { if (!isAdmin_(discordId)) return { status: 'error', message: '權限不足' }; var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SHEET_ID); var betSheet = ss.getSheetByName(GAMBLING_BET_SHEET_NAME); if (!betSheet) return { status: 'success', list: [] }; var betData = betSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); var playerData = ss.getSheets()[0].getDataRange().getValues(); var list = []; for (var b = 1; b < betData.length; b++) { if (!betData[b][0] || betData[b][0].toString() !== params.itemId.toString()) continue; var uid = betData[b][1] ? betData[b][1].toString().replace("'", "") : ''; if (!uid) continue; list.push({ discordId: uid, name: getPlayerDisplayName_(uid, ss, playerData) || uid, option: betData[b][2] ? betData[b][2].toString() : '', amount: parseFloat(betData[b][3]) || 0, }); } return { status: 'success', list: list }; } // 🌟 管理員手動公布賭博結果:選定哪個選項獲勝,系統依 FIXED(固定賠率)或 POOL(集資池)模式自動結算發放, // 輸家依商品設定的「輸家退還比例」發放退款(0=完全不退)。整場只能結算一次(結果寫進AU欄後就鎖住)。 function adminSettleGambling(discordId, params) { if (!isAdmin_(discordId)) return { status: 'error', message: '權限不足' }; var lock = LockService.getScriptLock(); lock.waitLock(20000); try { var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SHEET_ID); var shopSheet = ss.getSheets()[1]; var data = shopSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); var rowIdx = -1; for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) { if (data[i][18] && data[i][18].toString().trim() === params.itemId.toString()) { rowIdx = i + 1; break; } } if (rowIdx === -1) return { status: 'error', message: '找不到此商品' }; var row = data[rowIdx - 1]; var isGambling = row[42] ? row[42].toString().trim().toUpperCase() === 'TRUE' : false; if (!isGambling) return { status: 'error', message: '這不是賭博模式的商品' }; var existingResult = row[46] ? row[46].toString().trim() : ''; if (existingResult) return { status: 'error', message: '這場賭博已經公布過結果了,不能重複結算' }; var itemName = row[0]; var itemId = row[18].toString().trim(); var currencyName = row[13] ? row[13].toString().trim() : '升階2'; var oddsMode = row[43] ? row[43].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : 'FIXED'; if (oddsMode !== 'POOL') oddsMode = 'FIXED'; var optionsRaw = row[44] ? row[44].toString().trim() : ''; var loserRefundPercent = row[45] !== '' && row[45] !== undefined ? parseFloat(row[45]) : 0; if (!(loserRefundPercent >= 0)) loserRefundPercent = 0; if (loserRefundPercent > 100) loserRefundPercent = 100; var poolLockMode = row[47] ? row[47].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : 'FINAL'; if (poolLockMode !== 'BETTIME') poolLockMode = 'FINAL'; var optionsList = parseGamblingOptions_(optionsRaw); var winningOption = (params.winningOption || '').toString().trim(); var isSweep = (winningOption === '__SWEEP__'); // 🌟 通殺模式:管理員判定這場全部下注者都算輸,不發任何中獎金額(退還比例照樣適用) if (!isSweep) { var winningOptOK = false; for (var oi = 0; oi < optionsList.length; oi++) { if (optionsList[oi].name === winningOption) { winningOptOK = true; break; } } if (!winningOptOK) return { status: 'error', message: '找不到這個選項,請確認名稱是否正確' }; } var betSheet = ss.getSheetByName(GAMBLING_BET_SHEET_NAME); var betData = betSheet ? betSheet.getDataRange().getValues() : []; var bets = []; // {discordId, option, amount, oddsAmountProduct} for (var b = 1; b < betData.length; b++) { if (betData[b][0] && betData[b][0].toString() === itemId) { bets.push({ discordId: betData[b][1].toString().replace("'", ""), option: betData[b][2] ? betData[b][2].toString() : '', amount: parseFloat(betData[b][3]) || 0, oddsAmountProduct: parseFloat(betData[b][4]) || 0, // 🌟 集資池「以下注當下賠率為主」模式用,其他模式忽略這個值 }); } } if (bets.length === 0) { shopSheet.getRange(rowIdx, 47).setValue(JSON.stringify({ winningOption: winningOption, isSweep: isSweep, settledAt: new Date().toISOString(), payouts: [], note: '無人下注' })); try { queueWebhook_('🎲 賭博商品【' + itemName + '】已公布結果:' + (isSweep ? '通殺,無人中獎' : '「' + winningOption + '」獲勝') + ',但無人下注。'); } catch (e) {} return { status: 'success', message: '已公布結果(無人下注)' }; } var playerSheet = ss.getSheets()[0]; var playerData = playerSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); var playerHeaders = playerData[0]; var colIndex = playerHeaders.indexOf(currencyName); if (colIndex === -1) return { status: 'error', message: '系統錯誤:找不到貨幣欄位 [' + currencyName + ']' }; // 🌟 通殺模式:winners強制為空陣列,所有下注者(不管押哪個選項)全部算輸家,依退還比例處理(0%=莊家全拿) var winners = isSweep ? [] : bets.filter(function (bt) { return bt.option === winningOption; }); var losers = isSweep ? bets.slice() : bets.filter(function (bt) { return bt.option !== winningOption; }); var winnerTotalStake = 0; winners.forEach(function (w) { winnerTotalStake += w.amount; }); var loserTotalStake = 0; losers.forEach(function (l) { loserTotalStake += l.amount; }); var payouts = []; // {discordId, option, amount(下注金額), payout(實際拿到多少)} if (oddsMode === 'FIXED') { // 🌟 固定賠率:贏家 = 下注金額 x 賠率;輸家依退還比例拿回一部分(0=不退) var winOptCfg = null; for (var wo = 0; wo < optionsList.length; wo++) { if (optionsList[wo].name === winningOption) { winOptCfg = optionsList[wo]; break; } } var winOdds = winOptCfg ? winOptCfg.odds : 0; winners.forEach(function (w) { payouts.push({ discordId: w.discordId, option: w.option, amount: w.amount, payout: Math.floor(w.amount * winOdds) }); }); losers.forEach(function (l) { var refund = loserRefundPercent > 0 ? Math.floor(l.amount * loserRefundPercent / 100) : 0; payouts.push({ discordId: l.discordId, option: l.option, amount: l.amount, payout: refund }); }); } else if (poolLockMode === 'BETTIME') { // 🌟 集資池「以下注當下賠率為主」:每一筆下注在下注當下就已經算好、鎖定了賠率(存在 oddsAmountProduct 裡, // = 下注金額 x 當下隱含賠率),贏家直接發放這個累計值,不受之後池子變化影響;輸家依退還比例處理(邏輯同上) winners.forEach(function (w) { payouts.push({ discordId: w.discordId, option: w.option, amount: w.amount, payout: Math.floor(w.oddsAmountProduct) }); }); losers.forEach(function (l) { var refund = loserRefundPercent > 0 ? Math.floor(l.amount * loserRefundPercent / 100) : 0; payouts.push({ discordId: l.discordId, option: l.option, amount: l.amount, payout: refund }); }); } else { // 🌟 集資池「依最終結算總額計算」(標準模式):所有輸家的錢扣掉退還比例後,依贏家下注金額比例分配;贏家本金也拿回來 var refundFromLoserPool = loserTotalStake * (loserRefundPercent / 100); var distributablePool = loserTotalStake - refundFromLoserPool; winners.forEach(function (w) { var share = winnerTotalStake > 0 ? (w.amount / winnerTotalStake) * distributablePool : 0; payouts.push({ discordId: w.discordId, option: w.option, amount: w.amount, payout: Math.floor(w.amount + share) }); }); losers.forEach(function (l) { var refund = loserRefundPercent > 0 ? Math.floor(l.amount * loserRefundPercent / 100) : 0; payouts.push({ discordId: l.discordId, option: l.option, amount: l.amount, payout: refund }); }); } var historySheet = ss.getSheets()[2]; var historyDataForUpdate = historySheet.getDataRange().getValues(); // 🌟 整張只讀一次,等下用來回頭找每個人當初下注的那幾筆紀錄 var grantedCount = 0, totalPaidOut = 0; var gSyncTotalsByPlayer = {}; // 🌟 同一個人不管押了幾個不同選項、拿到幾種不同賠率的錢,結算後只發「一則」同步訊息,金額直接加總 payouts.forEach(function (p) { var isWin = p.option === winningOption; // 🌟🔧 回頭找這個人當初下注這個選項的歷史紀錄,把「是否中獎、實際拿到多少」同步標記回原本那幾筆。 // 這裡標記的金額是「這一筆下注自己」應得的金額,不是整個選項的彙總數字—— // 固定賠率/集資池下注當下鎖定模式,下注當時就已經算好且寫進這筆紀錄的「若中獎可得 X」,直接讀出來用最準; // 依最終結算總額模式沒有預先鎖定金額,退回用「這筆下注金額 ÷ 這個人在這個選項的總下注」比例去分攤彙總金額。 var betTag = '下注「' + p.option + '」'; for (var hr = 1; hr < historyDataForUpdate.length; hr++) { if (historyDataForUpdate[hr][4] && historyDataForUpdate[hr][4].toString() === itemId && historyDataForUpdate[hr][1] && historyDataForUpdate[hr][1].toString().replace("'", "") === p.discordId && historyDataForUpdate[hr][6] && historyDataForUpdate[hr][6].toString().indexOf(betTag) !== -1 && historyDataForUpdate[hr][6].toString().indexOf('已結算') === -1) { var rowText = historyDataForUpdate[hr][6].toString(); // 🌟 抓出這一筆下注自己的金額(格式:下注「選項」123 貨幣...) var rowAmountMatch = rowText.match(/下注「[^」]*」([\d.]+)\s/); var rowAmount = rowAmountMatch ? parseFloat(rowAmountMatch[1]) : p.amount; var rowOutcomeText; if (isWin) { // 🌟 優先讀取下注當時就算好寫在這筆紀錄裡的「若中獎可得 X」(固定賠率/下注當下鎖定模式都有) var potentialMatch = rowText.match(/若中獎可得\s*([\d.]+)/); var rowPayout; if (potentialMatch) { rowPayout = Math.floor(parseFloat(potentialMatch[1])); } else { // 🌟 依最終結算總額模式:下注當時沒有預先鎖定金額,改用「這筆金額佔這個人在這個選項總下注的比例」去分攤彙總金額 rowPayout = p.amount > 0 ? Math.floor((rowAmount / p.amount) * p.payout) : 0; } rowOutcomeText = ' → ✅ 已結算：中獎，此筆獲得 ' + rowPayout + ' ' + getDisplayCurrencyName_(currencyName); } else { var rowRefund = loserRefundPercent > 0 ? Math.floor(rowAmount * loserRefundPercent / 100) : 0; rowOutcomeText = rowRefund > 0 ? (' → ❌ 已結算：未中獎，此筆退還 ' + rowRefund + ' ' + getDisplayCurrencyName_(currencyName)) : ' → ❌ 已結算：未中獎，不退還'; } var newText = rowText + rowOutcomeText; historySheet.getRange(hr + 1, 7).setValue(newText); historyDataForUpdate[hr][6] = newText; // 更新記憶體副本,避免重複處理 } } if (p.payout <= 0) return; var pRow = -1; for (var pp = 1; pp < playerData.length; pp++) { if (playerData[pp][0].toString().replace("'", "") === p.discordId) { pRow = pp + 1; break; } } if (pRow === -1) { queueWebhook_('⚠️ 系統錯誤:賭博結算 <@' + p.discordId + '> 已不在玩家表中'); return; } var cur = parseInt(playerSheet.getRange(pRow, colIndex + 1).getValue()) || 0; playerSheet.getRange(pRow, colIndex + 1).setValue(cur + p.payout); grantedCount++; totalPaidOut += p.payout; // 🌟🔧 這裡先不急著發同步訊息,累加到這個人的總額裡,等全部處理完再「每人一則」統一發送, // 避免同一人押多個選項時,一次結算被拆成好幾則訊息(浪費訊息數量,也更容易踩到 Discord 限流) gSyncTotalsByPlayer[p.discordId] = (gSyncTotalsByPlayer[p.discordId] || 0) + p.payout; }); // 🌟 每人結算完成後只發一則同步訊息,把這個人不管押了幾個選項、各自賠率多少,全部加總成一個金額一起同步給 Skript var gSyncDisplayCurrency = getDisplayCurrencyName_(currencyName); Object.keys(gSyncTotalsByPlayer).forEach(function (pid) { var totalForPlayer = gSyncTotalsByPlayer[pid]; if (totalForPlayer <= 0) return; var gSyncMsg = "[購買] " + pid + " " + itemName + "|賭博結算 1 0 " + gSyncDisplayCurrency + " " + gSyncDisplayCurrency + " " + totalForPlayer; try { queueWebhook_(gSyncMsg); } catch (e) {} }); shopSheet.getRange(rowIdx, 47).setValue(JSON.stringify({ winningOption: winningOption, isSweep: isSweep, settledAt: new Date().toISOString(), payouts: payouts })); // 🌟 W(48)=結算完成時要不要順便公開廣播結果摘要(留空=不廣播,只做上面那些私訊/同步;TRUE=額外多發一則公開摘要公告) var gBroadcastOnSettle = row[48] ? row[48].toString().trim().toUpperCase() === 'TRUE' : false; if (gBroadcastOnSettle) { // 🌟 這裡用結構化格式送給瓜.sk(不是純文字),它才知道要把這則轉發到「大獎頻道」,並且能列出中獎名單。 // 格式:[賭博摘要] 商品名稱|獲勝選項(通殺時顯示「通殺」)|總下注筆數|發放筆數|總發放金額|貨幣顯示名稱|中獎者列表 // 中獎者列表 = "discordId:金額,discordId:金額,..."(只列真的贏錢拿到payout>0的人,通殺/沒人中就空字串) var gWinnerListStr = isSweep ? '' : payouts.filter(function (p) { return p.option === winningOption && p.payout > 0; }) .map(function (p) { return p.discordId + ':' + p.payout; }).join(','); var announceMsg = "[賭博摘要] " + itemName + "|" + (isSweep ? '通殺(全員未中獎)' : winningOption) + "|" + bets.length + "|" + grantedCount + "|" + totalPaidOut + "|" + getDisplayCurrencyName_(currencyName) + "|" + gWinnerListStr; try { queueWebhook_(announceMsg); } catch (e) {} } return { status: 'success', message: (isSweep ? '已通殺,全員未中獎，結算完成！' : '已公布結果並完成結算！'), payouts: payouts }; } finally { lock.releaseLock(); flushPendingWebhooks_(); } } // ============================================================ // 🌟 拍賣功能 // 工作表結構(需自己建立兩張表,名稱要跟上面 AUCTION_SHEET_NAME / BID_SHEET_NAME 一致): // // 「拍賣」工作表欄位 A~S(另有 T 狀態 / U 顯示順序 / V~Y 見下方抽獎相關欄位): // A 拍賣名稱 | B 起標價 | C 類型(PUBLIC公開比價/SEALED暗標/SEALED_LOW暗標低者得,預設PUBLIC) | D 結束時間 // E 延長觸發分鐘(最後幾分鐘內有出價就延長,留空=不延長) | F 延長分鐘數 // G 管理狀態(留空=進行中,填CLOSED=管理員手動關閉) | H 貨幣欄位名稱(對應玩家表,如 升階2) // I 圖片網址 | J 備註 | K 拍賣ID(系統自動產生,留空) | L 目前最高出價(系統寫入) // M 目前最高出價者DiscordID(系統寫入) | N 已結算(系統寫入,TRUE=已經處理完退款/發獎,避免重複結算) // O 限定身分組 | P 起標時間(留空=現在就能開始) | Q 分類 // R 替代貨幣欄位名稱(例如「拍賣幣」,留空=不開放折抵) | S 替代貨幣匯率(1個替代幣可折抵多少個原始貨幣) // // 🌟🎰 拍賣抽獎相關欄位(V~Y,選填,只對「暗標SEALED/SEALED_LOW」類型有意義——因為公開比價PUBLIC任何時刻 // 都只會留一筆凍結出價,沒有完整名單可以排名次或抽獎,設了也不會有效果): // V 得獎人數(前X名得獎,留空/1=一般單一得標者模式;填2以上=出價前X名各自付自己出的價格、都得標, // 等於一次賣出X份一樣的東西;金額互撞的算撞價淘汰,不計入贏家) // W 安慰獎抽獎名額(留空/0=不開放;填N=從「沒得標」的人裡面抽N位,每人機會均等不看出價金額, // 抽中的人不會重複抽兩次名額) // X 安慰獎獎池(留空=不開放;格式完全比照商店盲盒規則,可多獎項,自動發放貨幣/序號給抽中的人) // Y 安慰獎開獎結果(系統寫入,JSON,不用手動填,留空) // // 「拍賣出價紀錄」工作表欄位 A~F: // A 時間 | B 拍賣ID | C DiscordID | D 出價金額(總價值,含替代貨幣折抵的部分) | E 狀態(FROZEN凍結中/REFUNDED已退回/WON得標) // F 這筆出價用掉多少替代貨幣折抵(0/留空=沒使用折抵) // ============================================================ function getAuctions(discordId) { var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SHEET_ID); var auctionSheet = ss.getSheetByName(AUCTION_SHEET_NAME); if (!auctionSheet) return { "status": "success", "auctions": [], "categoryOrder": [] }; // 還沒建立拍賣功能,回傳空陣列不報錯 var data = auctionSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); var bidSheet = ss.getSheetByName(BID_SHEET_NAME); var bidData = bidSheet ? bidSheet.getDataRange().getValues() : []; var now = new Date().getTime(); var auctions = []; // 🌟 拍賣分類排序：讀「分類排序」工作表 B 欄(A 欄是商店分類,B 欄是拍賣分類) var auctionCategoryOrder = []; if (ss.getSheets().length >= 6) { var catSheet = ss.getSheets()[5]; var catData = catSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); for (var c = 1; c < catData.length; c++) { if (catData[c][1]) auctionCategoryOrder.push(catData[c][1].toString().trim()); } } var userRoles = getUserRoles(discordId, ss); // 🌟 身分組限定 var roleMap = getGuildRoleMap(ss); var playerSheetForNames = ss.getSheets()[0]; var playerDataForNames = playerSheetForNames.getDataRange().getValues(); // 🌟 公開拍賣要顯示出價者暱稱用 var playerHeadersForAlt = playerDataForNames[0]; var playerRowForAlt = -1; for (var pa = 1; pa < playerDataForNames.length; pa++) { if (playerDataForNames[pa][0] && playerDataForNames[pa][0].toString().replace("'", "") === discordId.toString()) { playerRowForAlt = pa; break; } } function getAuctionAltBalance_(altCurrencyName) { if (!altCurrencyName || playerRowForAlt === -1) return 0; var colIdx = playerHeadersForAlt.indexOf(altCurrencyName); if (colIdx === -1) return 0; return parseInt(playerDataForNames[playerRowForAlt][colIdx]) || 0; } for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) { var name = data[i][0] ? data[i][0].toString() : ''; // 🌟🔧 強制轉字串:商品名稱如果剛好是純數字(例如「88」),Google Sheets會自動存成數字型態,後面的.indexOf()是字串專用方法,不轉型會直接炸掉整個列表 if (!name) continue; var draftStatus = data[i][19] ? data[i][19].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : ''; // T(19) 狀態:DRAFT=草稿,不對玩家顯示 if (draftStatus === 'DRAFT') continue; var auctionId = data[i][10] ? data[i][10].toString().trim() : ''; if (!auctionId) { auctionId = Utilities.getUuid().split('-')[0].toUpperCase(); auctionSheet.getRange(i + 1, 11).setValue(auctionId); } var startBid = parseInt(data[i][1]) || 0; var type = (data[i][2] || 'PUBLIC').toString().trim().toUpperCase(); if (type !== 'SEALED' && type !== 'SEALED_LOW') type = 'PUBLIC'; // 🌟 SEALED_LOW = 暗標,但出價最低者得標 var endDate = dateColTime_(data[i][3]); var extendTriggerMin = data[i][4] !== '' && data[i][4] !== undefined ? parseInt(data[i][4]) : null; // E(4) 延長觸發分鐘 var extendByMin = data[i][5] !== '' && data[i][5] !== undefined ? parseInt(data[i][5]) : null; // F(5) 延長分鐘數 var manualStatus = data[i][6] ? data[i][6].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : ''; var currencyName = data[i][7] ? data[i][7].toString().trim() : '升階2'; var displayCurrency = (currencyName === '升階2') ? '幻彩水晶' : currencyName; var imageUrl = data[i][8] ? data[i][8].toString().trim() : ''; var remark = data[i][9] ? data[i][9].toString().trim() : ''; var currentHighBid = data[i][11] !== '' && data[i][11] !== undefined ? parseInt(data[i][11]) : startBid; var currentHighBidder = data[i][12] ? data[i][12].toString().trim() : ''; var settled = (data[i][13] === true || data[i][13] === 'TRUE'); var requiredRoleStr = data[i][14] ? data[i][14].toString().trim() : ''; // O(14) 🌟 限定身分組 var startDate = dateColTime_(data[i][15]); // P(15) 🌟 起標時間,留空=現在就能開始 var category = data[i][16] ? data[i][16].toString().trim() : '未分類'; // Q(16) 🌟 分類 // 🌟 替代貨幣折抵(例如拍賣幣):R(17)=替代貨幣欄位名稱, S(18)=匯率(1個替代幣可折抵多少個原始貨幣) var altCurrency = data[i][17] ? data[i][17].toString().trim() : ''; var altCurrencyRate = data[i][18] !== '' && data[i][18] !== undefined ? parseFloat(data[i][18]) : 0; if (!(altCurrencyRate > 0)) altCurrency = ''; var altCurrencyBalance = altCurrency ? getAuctionAltBalance_(altCurrency) : 0; var isNotStarted = (startDate && now < startDate); var isEnded = !isNotStarted && ((manualStatus === 'CLOSED') || (endDate && now > endDate)); var requiredRoleNames = []; var roleRequirementMode = 'ANY', roleRequirementMinCount = 1; if (requiredRoleStr) { var roleReq = parseRoleRequirement(requiredRoleStr); roleRequirementMode = roleReq.mode; roleRequirementMinCount = roleReq.minCount; for (var rI = 0; rI < roleReq.ids.length; rI++) requiredRoleNames.push(roleMap[roleReq.ids[rI]] || ('未知身分組' + roleReq.ids[rI])); } var hasRolePermission = checkRolePermission(userRoles, requiredRoleStr); // 找這個玩家在這場拍賣裡,目前還生效(FROZEN)的出價金額,給前端顯示「您目前出價」用 var myActiveBid = null; var myActiveBidAlt = 0; for (var b = bidData.length - 1; b >= 1; b--) { if (bidData[b][1] && bidData[b][1].toString() === auctionId && bidData[b][2] && bidData[b][2].toString().replace("'", "") === discordId.toString() && bidData[b][4] === 'FROZEN') { myActiveBid = parseInt(bidData[b][3]) || 0; myActiveBidAlt = bidData[b][5] !== '' && bidData[b][5] !== undefined ? (parseInt(bidData[b][5]) || 0) : 0; break; } } var state; if (isNotStarted) state = 'not_started'; else if (isEnded) state = settled ? 'ended' : 'pending_settlement'; else if (!hasRolePermission) state = 'no_permission'; else state = 'open'; // 🌟 公開比價模式才公布出價者名稱(暗標模式繼續保密,不洩漏身分) var currentHighBidderName = null; if (type === 'PUBLIC' && currentHighBidder !== '' && currentHighBidder !== discordId.toString()) { currentHighBidderName = getPlayerDisplayName_(currentHighBidder, ss, playerDataForNames) || ('玩家' + currentHighBidder.slice(-4)); } // 🌟 前X名得獎模式底下,「我是不是贏家」要看出價紀錄裡有沒有被標記WON,不能只看currentHighBidder(那只代表排名最高的1位) var myWonThisAuction = false; for (var bw = 1; bw < bidData.length; bw++) { if (bidData[bw][1] && bidData[bw][1].toString() === auctionId && bidData[bw][2] && bidData[bw][2].toString().replace("'", "") === discordId.toString() && bidData[bw][4] === 'WON') { myWonThisAuction = true; break; } } // 🌟 V(21)得獎人數 | W(22)安慰獎名額 | Y(24)安慰獎結果(系統寫入) var winnerCount = data[i][21] !== '' && data[i][21] !== undefined ? parseInt(data[i][21]) : 1; if (!(winnerCount >= 1)) winnerCount = 1; var raffleSlots = data[i][22] !== '' && data[i][22] !== undefined ? parseInt(data[i][22]) : 0; var raffleResultRaw = data[i][24] ? data[i][24].toString().trim() : ''; var raffleWinnersList = raffleResultRaw ? safeParseJSON_(raffleResultRaw) : null; var myRafflePrize = null; if (raffleWinnersList) { for (var rw = 0; rw < raffleWinnersList.length; rw++) { if (raffleWinnersList[rw].discordId === discordId.toString()) { myRafflePrize = raffleWinnersList[rw].prize; break; } } } auctions.push({ id: auctionId, name: name, type: type, startBid: startBid, startDate: startDate, endDate: endDate, currencyName: currencyName, displayCurrency: displayCurrency, imageUrl: imageUrl, remark: remark, state: state, currentHighBid: type === 'PUBLIC' ? currentHighBid : null, // 暗標模式不公開目前最高價 currentHighBidderName: currentHighBidderName, // 🌟 公開拍賣的目前最高出價者暱稱 hasAnyBid: currentHighBidder !== '', currentHighBidderIsMe: currentHighBidder !== '' && currentHighBidder === discordId.toString(), myActiveBid: myActiveBid, myActiveBidAlt: myActiveBidAlt, winnerIsMe: isEnded && settled && myWonThisAuction, winningBid: (isEnded && settled && currentHighBidder !== '') ? currentHighBid : null, requiredRoleNames: requiredRoleNames, hasRolePermission: hasRolePermission, roleRequirementMode: roleRequirementMode, roleRequirementMinCount: roleRequirementMinCount, category: category, // 🌟 分類 altCurrency: altCurrency, altCurrencyRate: altCurrencyRate, altCurrencyBalance: altCurrencyBalance, // 🌟 替代貨幣折抵資訊 extendTriggerMin: extendTriggerMin, extendByMin: extendByMin, // 🌟 自動延長規則(最後N分鐘內有人出價,就延長M分鐘) winnerCount: winnerCount, // 🌟 前X名得獎(=1代表一般單一得標者模式) raffleSlots: raffleSlots, // 🌟 安慰獎抽獎名額(0=沒開放) raffleDrawn: !!raffleResultRaw, // 🌟 安慰獎是否已經開獎過 myRafflePrize: myRafflePrize, // 🌟 我是否中了安慰獎、中了什麼(沒中是 null) }); } return { "status": "success", "auctions": auctions, "categoryOrder": auctionCategoryOrder }; } function placeBid(discordId, auctionId, bidAmount, altMode, altAmountParam) { var lock = LockService.getScriptLock(); lock.waitLock(15000); try { bidAmount = parseInt(bidAmount) || 0; if (bidAmount <= 0) return { "status": "error", "message": "出價金額不正確" }; altMode = altMode || 'none'; var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SHEET_ID); var auctionSheet = ss.getSheetByName(AUCTION_SHEET_NAME); if (!auctionSheet) return { "status": "error", "message": "尚未設定拍賣功能" }; var auctionData = auctionSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); var rowIdx = -1; for (var i = 1; i < auctionData.length; i++) { if (auctionData[i][10] && auctionData[i][10].toString().trim() === auctionId.toString()) { rowIdx = i; break; } } if (rowIdx === -1) return { "status": "error", "message": "找不到這場拍賣" }; var row = auctionData[rowIdx]; var name = row[0]; var startBid = parseInt(row[1]) || 0; var type = (row[2] || 'PUBLIC').toString().trim().toUpperCase(); if (type !== 'SEALED' && type !== 'SEALED_LOW') type = 'PUBLIC'; // 🌟 SEALED_LOW = 暗標,但出價最低者得標 var endDate = dateColTime_(row[3]); var extendTriggerMin = row[4] !== '' && row[4] !== undefined ? parseInt(row[4]) : null; var extendByMin = row[5] !== '' && row[5] !== undefined ? parseInt(row[5]) : null; var manualStatus = row[6] ? row[6].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : ''; var currencyName = row[7] ? row[7].toString().trim() : '升階2'; var displayCurrencyName = (currencyName === '升階2') ? '幻彩水晶' : currencyName; var currentHighBid = row[11] !== '' && row[11] !== undefined ? parseInt(row[11]) : startBid; var currentHighBidder = row[12] ? row[12].toString().trim() : ''; var settled = (row[13] === true || row[13] === 'TRUE'); var requiredRoleStr = row[14] ? row[14].toString().trim() : ''; // O(14) 🌟 限定身分組 var startDate = dateColTime_(row[15]); // P(15) 🌟 起標時間 var draftStatus = row[19] ? row[19].toString().trim().toUpperCase() : ''; // T(19) 狀態:DRAFT=草稿 // 🌟 替代貨幣折抵(例如拍賣幣):R(17)=替代貨幣欄位名稱, S(18)=匯率(1個替代幣可折抵多少個原始貨幣) var altCurrencyName = row[17] ? row[17].toString().trim() : ''; var altCurrencyRate = row[18] !== '' && row[18] !== undefined ? parseFloat(row[18]) : 0; if (!(altCurrencyRate > 0)) altCurrencyName = ''; var now = new Date().getTime(); if (draftStatus === 'DRAFT') return { "status": "error", "message": "此拍賣尚未上架(草稿狀態)" }; if (startDate && now < startDate) return { "status": "error", "message": "拍賣尚未開始" }; if (settled || manualStatus === 'CLOSED') return { "status": "error", "message": "此拍賣已經結束" }; if (endDate && now > endDate) return { "status": "error", "message": "此拍賣已經結束" }; // 🌟 身分組限定檢查：後端再驗證一次,避免前端被繞過 if (requiredRoleStr) { var userRolesForBidCheck = getUserRoles(discordId, ss); if (!checkRolePermission(userRolesForBidCheck, requiredRoleStr)) { var roleMapForBidCheck = getGuildRoleMap(ss); var roleReqForBidCheck = parseRoleRequirement(requiredRoleStr); var reqNamesForBid = roleReqForBidCheck.ids.map(function(id) { return roleMapForBidCheck[id] || id; }); var reqHintForBid = ""; if (roleReqForBidCheck.mode === 'ALL') reqHintForBid = "需全部持有："; else if (roleReqForBidCheck.mode === 'COUNT') reqHintForBid = "需持有其中至少 " + roleReqForBidCheck.minCount + " 個："; else reqHintForBid = "需持有其中任一個："; return { "status": "error", "message": "您沒有出價此拍賣所需的身分組(" + reqHintForBid + reqNamesForBid.join("、") + ")" }; } } if (type === 'PUBLIC') { if (currentHighBidder === '') { if (bidAmount < startBid) return { "status": "error", "message": "出價不能低於起標價 " + startBid }; } else if (currentHighBidder !== discordId.toString() && bidAmount <= currentHighBid) { return { "status": "error", "message": "出價必須高於目前最高出價 " + currentHighBid }; } else if (currentHighBidder === discordId.toString() && bidAmount <= currentHighBid) { return { "status": "error", "message": "您已經是目前最高出價者(" + currentHighBid + "),新出價必須更高" }; } } else if (type === 'SEALED_LOW') { // 暗標(低者得):彼此看不到對方出多少,只要求不高於起標價(起標價當作上限) if (bidAmount > startBid) return { "status": "error", "message": "出價不能高於起標價(上限) " + startBid }; } else { // SEALED 暗標(高者得):彼此看不到對方出多少,只要求不低於起標價 if (bidAmount < startBid) return { "status": "error", "message": "出價不能低於起標價 " + startBid }; } var playerSheet = ss.getSheets()[0]; var playerData = playerSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); var playerHeaders = playerData[0]; var colIndex = playerHeaders.indexOf(currencyName); if (colIndex === -1) return { "status": "error", "message": "系統錯誤:找不到貨幣欄位[" + currencyName + "]" }; var playerRow = -1, currentBalance = 0; for (var p = 1; p < playerData.length; p++) { if (playerData[p][0].toString().replace("'", "") === discordId.toString()) { playerRow = p + 1; currentBalance = parseInt(playerData[p][colIndex]) || 0; break; } } if (playerRow === -1) return { "status": "error", "message": "找不到您的帳號資料" }; // 🌟 替代貨幣欄位存在性檢查、以及玩家目前的替代幣餘額(要在真的開始扣款前就確認好) var altColIndex = -1, altBalance = 0; if (altCurrencyName && altMode !== 'none') { altColIndex = playerHeaders.indexOf(altCurrencyName); if (altColIndex === -1) return { "status": "error", "message": "系統錯誤：找不到替代貨幣欄位 [" + altCurrencyName + "]" }; altBalance = parseInt(playerData[playerRow - 1][altColIndex]) || 0; } var bidSheet = ss.getSheetByName(BID_SHEET_NAME); if (!bidSheet) return { "status": "error", "message": "尚未建立「拍賣出價紀錄」工作表" }; var bidData = bidSheet.getDataRange().getValues(); if (type === 'PUBLIC') { // 公開比價:任何時刻只有「目前最高出價者」的錢被凍結著,新出價進來時把舊的最高出價者退款 if (currentHighBidder !== '') { var isSelfRaisePublic = (currentHighBidder === discordId.toString()); var refundResult = refundActiveBid_(playerSheet, playerData, playerHeaders, colIndex, currentHighBidder, currentHighBid, bidSheet, bidData, auctionId, name, currencyName, isSelfRaisePublic, altCurrencyName, altCurrencyRate, discordId, bidAmount); if (isSelfRaisePublic) { currentBalance += refundResult.mainRefunded; // 退的剛好是自己,餘額要跟著加回來 altBalance += refundResult.altRefunded; // 替代幣也是,退回的要加回自己剛剛讀到的餘額 } } var altAmountUsed = computeAltUsage_(bidAmount, altBalance, altCurrencyRate, altMode, altAmountParam); if (altAmountUsed.error) return { "status": "error", "message": altAmountUsed.error }; var mainNeeded = altAmountUsed.mainNeeded; // 🌟 替代貨幣欄位剛好跟主要貨幣欄位一樣的情況,兩者要合併判斷/合併扣款,避免互相蓋掉 if (altColIndex !== -1 && altColIndex === colIndex) { if (currentBalance < mainNeeded + altAmountUsed.used) return { "status": "error", "message": displayCurrencyName + " 不足,無法出價" }; playerSheet.getRange(playerRow, colIndex + 1).setValue(currentBalance - mainNeeded - altAmountUsed.used); } else { if (currentBalance < mainNeeded) return { "status": "error", "message": displayCurrencyName + " 不足,無法出價" }; playerSheet.getRange(playerRow, colIndex + 1).setValue(currentBalance - mainNeeded); if (altAmountUsed.used > 0) playerSheet.getRange(playerRow, altColIndex + 1).setValue(altBalance - altAmountUsed.used); } sendAuctionBidWebhook_(discordId, name, mainNeeded, currencyName, altAmountUsed.used > 0 ? altCurrencyName : '', altAmountUsed.used); auctionSheet.getRange(rowIdx + 1, 12, 1, 2).setValues([[bidAmount, "'" + discordId.toString()]]); // 🌟 L/M兩欄合併成一次寫入 bidSheet.appendRow([new Date(), auctionId, "'" + discordId.toString(), bidAmount, 'FROZEN', altAmountUsed.used]); } else { // 暗標:每個人各自獨立凍結,彼此不會互相退款,要等結標才一次處理; // 如果這個人對「同一場」拍賣重複出價,視為「覆蓋上一次出價」,先退回自己舊的再扣新的 var prevBid = findActiveBid_(bidData, auctionId, discordId); if (prevBid) { var selfRefund = refundActiveBid_(playerSheet, playerData, playerHeaders, colIndex, discordId, prevBid.amount, bidSheet, bidData, auctionId, name, currencyName, true, altCurrencyName, altCurrencyRate); currentBalance += selfRefund.mainRefunded; altBalance += selfRefund.altRefunded; } var altAmountUsedSealed = computeAltUsage_(bidAmount, altBalance, altCurrencyRate, altMode, altAmountParam); if (altAmountUsedSealed.error) return { "status": "error", "message": altAmountUsedSealed.error }; var mainNeededSealed = altAmountUsedSealed.mainNeeded; if (altColIndex !== -1 && altColIndex === colIndex) { if (currentBalance < mainNeededSealed + altAmountUsedSealed.used) return { "status": "error", "message": displayCurrencyName + " 不足,無法出價" }; playerSheet.getRange(playerRow, colIndex + 1).setValue(currentBalance - mainNeededSealed - altAmountUsedSealed.used); } else { if (currentBalance < mainNeededSealed) return { "status": "error", "message": displayCurrencyName + " 不足,無法出價" }; playerSheet.getRange(playerRow, colIndex + 1).setValue(currentBalance - mainNeededSealed); if (altAmountUsedSealed.used > 0) playerSheet.getRange(playerRow, altColIndex + 1).setValue(altBalance - altAmountUsedSealed.used); } sendAuctionBidWebhook_(discordId, name, mainNeededSealed, currencyName, altAmountUsedSealed.used > 0 ? altCurrencyName : '', altAmountUsedSealed.used); // 暗標模式仍要偷偷記下目前領先出價(只是不顯示給玩家看),結標時要靠這個判斷贏家 // 🌟 SEALED(高者得):出價越高越領先；SEALED_LOW(低者得):出價越低越領先 var isLeadingBid = (currentHighBidder === '') || (type === 'SEALED_LOW' ?
